    "課程大綱": "Title: 從心理學看成功老化PSYCHOLOGICAL APPROACH TO SUCCESSFUL AGING 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A92U200&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n本課程旨在從心理學的角度介紹老化的過程，針對成功老化之經典學說和理論、對老年人的刻板印象、老年期將經歷之變化（包含身心健康、認知、社會關係、親密關係等），以及死亡關懷等議題進行討論。課程內容透過理解老年期之生理、心理、認知之變化和社會行為與調適等，探討老化的歷程及影響。透過心理科學研究和實例之結合，讓學生更全面了解步入老年期的狀態、挑戰及因應之道。本課程除了協助學生更認識老化的歷程與實用知識，也期待以正向老化的思維引導，提供學生一個自助或助人之參考。  \nThis course is aimed to offer students an introduction and overview of the aging process from a psychological standpoint, with a particular emphasis on theories of successful aging, stereotypes about aging and older adults, changes in physical and mental health, cognition, personal transitions in later life, social relationships and sexuality in later life, and death and dying. The interaction of aging, physiological changes, cognitive changes, psychological changes, and society, as well as how the effects of aging affect behavior, will be the underlying theme throughout the course. Scientific data and real-life examples will be amalgamated to form a more comprehensive picture of what it is like to be an older adult in the twenty-first century. The goal of this course is for students to not only gain a better understanding of aging, but also to learn how to age successfully themselves.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   Explain the basic fundamentals of the psychology of aging\n*   Conceptualize later life as part of a developmental process\n*   Comprehend and apply the empirical literature dealing with aging\n*   Promote positive attitudes toward aging and elders\n*   Prepare students to successfully age themselves\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Course Introduction – Review of syllabus |\n| 2 | Themes and Issues in Adult Development and Aging |\n| 3 | Models of Development: Nature and Nurture in Adulthood |\n| 4 | Health and Prevention |\n| 5 | Double Tenth Holiday (No class) |\n| 6 | Basic Cognitive Functions: Information Processing, Attention, and Memory |\n| 7 | Personality |\n| 8 | Quiz 1 |\n| 9 | Relationships/Introduction to Final Project Guidelines |\n| 10 | Films about Aging |\n| 11 | Mental Health Issues and Treatment |\n| 12 | Long-Term Care/Death and Dying |\n| 13 | Successful Aging/Quiz Review Session |\n| 14 | Quiz 2/Final Presentation Preparation Session |\n| 15 | Student Final Presentations |\n| 16 | Student Final Presentations |\n| 17 | Student Final Presentations |\n| 18 | Final Essay Preparation Week |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? As Steven Jobs said “People don’t know what they want until you show them.” A good DataViz design, according to my opinion, is a design that can express what people want and could not been expressed by themselves. Please actively participate this course and you can make it.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   Select “proper” graphs (charts) and visual properties according to question.\n*   Create DataViz dashboards with some functions such as self-selection.\n*   Create a series of story boards and interactive cloud slides.\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Purpose of DataViz: (1) to quickly find out known answers for known questions; (2) to self-sect the benchmarks to find out the unknown problems |\n| 2 | Commonly used indicators in DataViz dashboards |\n| 3 | What is your point (value judgement or conclusion) in a graph or chart? |\n| 4 | Putting the same data in different contexts to produce different value judgement (information or conclusion) |\n| 5 | How to select proper graphs or charts according to the purpose and scale (level) of measurement of the data? |\n| 6 | How to select proper visual properties according to the purpose and scale (level) of measurement of the data? |\n| 7 | Student presentation of good DataViz dashboards to illustrated how the designers used different skills to highlight the points (several weeks) |\n| 8 | Learning the basic skills of self-service business intelligent software (Tableau) |\n| 9 | How to create a story? |\n| 10 | Student presentation of good DataViz dashboards stories |\n| 11 | Student presentation of his/her idea of modifications |\n| 12 | 講故事\\_見林見樹見葉Story telling: From forests to trees |\n| 13 | 講故事\\_阻礙與突破Story telling: barriers and overcome |\n| 14 | 講故事\\_阻礙與突破Story telling: barriers and overcome |\n| 15 | 資訊圖表\\_1 Infographics\\_2 |\n| 16 | 資訊圖表\\_2 Infographics\\_2 |\n| 17 | 期末報告：同學視覺化作品分享Final term report：Students presenting their DataViz works |\n| 18 | 期末報告：同學視覺化作品分享Final term report：Students presenting their DataViz works |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? It focuses on the ecology, phenomena and problems of Taiwanese media and instructs students to explore the role that media plays in daily life, public sphere and public interests. In addition, some simple and feasible Chinese medicine diet therapy formulas are also introduced. The first half of the course included basic theories, physique discrimination, the taste and function of herbs. The latter part illustrates the principle of dietary preparation, the choice of medicinal materials, and precautions for cooking, together with basic nutritional knowledge to illustrate the effects of dietary therapy. Students are expected to learn how to improve the living habits and health of themselves or their family members.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解中醫食療的基礎理論\n*   學習選擇簡單可行的食療藥膳方\n*   培養學生對藥膳食療的興趣\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 緒論 |\n| 2 | 中醫藥與中醫食療/基礎理論常識 |\n| 3 | 中醫藥與中醫食療/基礎理論常識 |\n| 4 | 食療的製作 |\n| 5 | 季節食療 |\n| 6 | 不同年齡食療 |\n| 7 | 美容食療和心能量 |\n| 8 | 常見病症之中醫食療/感冒、發燒、鼻炎 |\n| 9 | 期中考/分組 |\n| 10 | 常見病症之中醫食療/胃腸病 |\n| 11 | 常見病症之中醫食療/婦科疾病 |\n| 12 | 常見病症之中醫食療/高血壓、糖尿病、三高 |\n| 13 | 常見病症之中醫食療/肝炎、腎病、男性疾病 |\n| 14 | 藥膳製作報告 |\n| 15 | 藥膳製作報告 |\n| 16 | 期末報告 |\n| 17 | 期末報告 |\n| 18 | 討論週 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? It is intended to be practical for clinicians and for researchers' reference. Therefore, this course is widely used in ancient and modern Chinese medicine literature, including Chinese traditional medicine and Japanese Han medicine, deeply aware of its origins, generations of development, very rich. Trying to organize and compile its most distinctive and practical content, and focus on the clinical experience that is still commonly used to guide clinical practice.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   中藥之外觀辦別\n*   中藥之方劑、用途介紹\n*   中藥對於疾病治療、藥膳及養生之藥理介紹\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 中藥之基本特性簡介 |\n| 2 | 各種中藥方劑的藥材介紹，藥效解說。 |\n| 3 | 與西洋醫藥的使用區別、併用、禁忌。 |\n| 4 | 呼吸系統用藥介紹 |\n| 5 | 消化系統用藥介紹 |\n| 6 | 消化系統用藥介紹 |\n| 7 | 循環系統用藥介紹 |\n| 8 | 循環系統用藥介紹 |\n| 9 | 期中考 |\n| 10 | 代謝系統用藥介紹 |\n| 11 | 代謝系統用藥介紹 |\n| 12 | 泌尿系統用藥介紹 |\n| 13 | 泌尿系統用藥介紹 |\n| 14 | 婦產科系統用藥介紹 |\n| 15 | 婦產科系統用藥介紹 |\n| 16 | 老人科系統用藥介紹 |\n| 17 | 老人科系統用藥介紹 |\n| 18 | 期末考 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   就業與經濟成長 (Decent work and Economic growth)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? In this lecture, we will introduce different levels of life sciences from molecules, cells, tissues, organs, systems, organisms, community to ecosystems. The background knowledge will include evolution, structure, function, underlying physiological and biochemistry mechanisms, and their interactions with biotic and abiotic environments. In addition, we will introduce some hot topics such as cancer metabolism, biotech and bioethics, climate change and plastic particles.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   從分子、細胞、有機體、物種及行為的層次，認識生命的起源及相關科學的最新發展\n*   認識生命、與瞭解自己與地球上其它生物的相關性\n*   愛護我們生活的地球，並珍惜地球上所有的生命\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   氣候行動 (Climate action)\n*   海洋生態 (Life below water)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? 說明問題解決的常用流程、介紹時間管理的概念與相關作法 第十一週：問題解決與時間管理 第十二週：睡眠、飲食與運動; 介紹睡眠、飲食、運動與身心健康的關係 第十三週：睡眠、飲食與運動 第十四週：正向的人生觀; 介紹後現代思潮對人的不同觀點，並討論這些觀點對人的影響 第十五週：正向的人生觀 第十六週：主題影片討論1 第十七週：主題影片討論2 第十八週：總結  \nWeek 1: Introduction to the course; Check-in, course description, other recommendations Week 2: Emotion, stress and physical and mental health; Explain emotions, stress-related patterns and their relationship to physical and mental health Week 3: Self-hypnosis and muscle relaxation; Explain self Hypnosis and muscle relaxation techniques, precautions, and exercises for the fourth week: Self-hypnosis and muscle relaxation Week 5: Physiological feedback skills; Explain the theoretical basis and practice of physiological feedback techniques, and conduct exercises for the sixth week: Physiological feedback Skills Week 7: Emotional Management I: REBT; If people do not possess the correct knowledge of medication use, it will greatly affect the effectiveness of disease treatment. This course aims to enhance students' awareness of medication therapy through case discussions, self or family medication reviews, visits to community pharmacies, and participation in community health education programs. By instilling correct medication knowledge from a young age, it can also influence the older generation at home. This not only enhances health literacy and promotes self-health management but also reduces the use of medical resources and the risk of mortality.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   完成本課程後學生會應用正確用藥五大核心能力\n*   完成本課程後學生會認識常見的藥物副作用與處理方式\n*   完成本課程後學生會了解如何正確獲取治療藥物的相關資訊\n*   完成本課程後學生會知道藥師可以提供的藥事照護\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介/藥師大解密-1 |\n| 2 | 課程簡介/藥師大解密-2 |\n| 3 | 我到底吃進了什麼？-1 |\n| 4 | 我到底吃進了什麼？-2 |\n| 5 | 我到底吃進了什麼？-3 |\n| 6 | 天呀，吃了怎麼變這樣!-1 |\n| 7 | 天呀，吃了怎麼變這樣!-2 |\n| 8 | 誰是用藥常識王？-1 |\n| 9 | 誰是用藥常識王？-2 |\n| 10 | 藥品磨粉比較好吞? |\n| 11 | 原來藥品也有分級? |\n| 12 | 連鎖藥局賣什麼？ |\n| 13 | 們的好厝邊-社區藥局 |\n| 14 | 我有三高會怎樣? |\n| 15 | 阿公阿嬤看過來！ |\n| 16 | 你會Hospital shopping嗎？ |\n| 17 | 藥師的社區關懷與衛教-1 |\n| 18 | 藥師的社區關懷與衛教-2 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 6 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 急難救助FIRST AID IN EMERGENCY 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A963002&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n鑑於國人休旅生活時間的延長與各類活動的多樣性，其中潛藏有不少的危險。因此緊急狀況中的處理能力顯得日益重要。本課程依急診醫學的內涵，以專業醫學相關之知識、技能並重，配合特殊緊急狀況下之處理原則等為教學內容。舉凡事故發生之預防、潛在危險事件的認知、事故發生後求援管道的連繫與初步處理、以及安全轉送的方法，均是同學應該具備的現代生活基本知識。除了知識教授外，也輔以實地體驗。山難、中暑、潛水病，毒蛇咬傷，中毒等等因特殊環境導致的各類急難情況以及從地球村的觀念探討全球氣候變遷、新興傳染症流行與國際人道救援衍生的急難議題。  \nIn view of the extension of the leisure time of the Chinese people and the diversity of various activities, there are many hidden dangers. Therefore, the processing power in emergencies is becoming increasingly important. This course is based on the connotation of emergency medicine, with the knowledge and skills related to professional medicine, and the handling principles under special emergency conditions. The prevention of accidents, the recognition of potential dangerous events, the connection and preliminary treatment of the aid pipeline after the accident, and the method of safe transfer are all basic knowledge of modern life that students should have. In addition to knowledge professors, it is complemented by field experience. It depends on its host for survival. In this course, the learning must learn the definition, original, history, importances, infection routes, such as fece-oral, food borne, waterborne, soil transmitted, zoonotic, and opportunistic, special topics, such as mosquito and cockroach, and future of human parasites. The teaching and evaluating methods are lectures, watching clips and several reports. After this course, we hope the students, they can recognize and have their own stories about parasites around us.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解感染寄生蟲對動物或人所造成的危害\n*   了解各種寄生蟲的感染途徑\n*   了解台灣寄生蟲病的研究現狀與未來\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹 |\n| 2 | 伊甸園的故事 |\n| 3 | 寄生蟲家族 |\n| 4 | 親密的敵人 |\n| 5 | 形形色色的寄生蟲 |\n| 6 | 歷史上的寄生蟲 |\n| 7 | 記憶中的寄生蟲 |\n| 8 | 赤足踩在田埂上 |\n| 9 | 病從口入 |\n| 10 | 吸血鬼的故事 |\n| 11 | 犬八與你 |\n| 12 | 蟲蟲就在你身邊 |\n| 13 | 疾病與媒介 |\n| 14 | 蟑螂Ｘ檔案 |\n| 15 | 自主學習：歷史的聲音（一） |\n| 16 | 自主學習：歷史的聲音（二） |\n| 17 | 自主學習：歷史的聲音（三） |\n| 18 | 寄生蟲學的下一步 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   消除貧窮 (No poverty)\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Human anatomy is generally studied by looking at the many and varied organs of the body. Most of these can be grouped together into different systems on the basis of those organs and their accompanying structures that work together to perform specific body functions. An extension of anatomy, physiology is concerned with how the various parts of the body work. However, because the structure of an organ or other unit is closely related to its function (role), anatomy and physiology are very closely related. The understand how the different organs link up, the body is studied in systems-groups of organs that work together. The organs in a system are grouped together not only because they are interconnected, but also because they contain the same type, or types of tissue. To understand different system or organs dysfunction or disorders and clarify common health misunderstanding. Moreover, how to visit hospital for preventive medicine, such as health promotion, self-physical checkup and early prevention of common disease and early treatment.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   學習跨領域的基礎知識\n*   養成因應新事務與學習新知的能力\n*   成為現代社會的健全公民\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 總論－人體之奧秘與身體之照顧 |\n| 2 | 第一道防線－皮膚 |\n| 3 | 內分泌─腦下垂體、腎上腺、甲狀腺 |\n| 4 | 糖尿病知多少? |\n| 5 | 胃腸消化道─營養吸收及廢物排泄 |\n| 6 | 耳聰目明--談眼睛及耳朵 |\n| 7 | 心臟、血管─自來〝血〞廠 |\n| 8 | 肺臟─空調系統 |\n| 9 | 肝膽相照話心肝寶貝 |\n| 10 | 校慶 |\n| 11 | 腎臟及泌尿系統─下水道 |\n| 12 | 血液淋巴─造血與防衛 |\n| 13 | 週期性健康檢查及自我檢查 |\n| 14 | 腦與神經─控制連絡中心 |\n| 15 | 活動筋骨永不生病－談肌肉骨骼系統 |\n| 16 | 生殖系統─綿延不絕 |\n| 17 | 考試準備週 |\n| 18 | 期末測驗 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? DNA如何操控著所有的生命活動? 基因改造又是甚麼?本課程將讓學生了解基因是甚麼，以及其背後隱藏的秘密。另一方面，也透過課程讓學生了解生物科技其實是一跨領域的科學，舉凡資訊、統計、數學、物理、化學等等都是協助解開基因密碼的利器。本課程除了透過老師講授之外，也將利用教學視聽資料(列於參考書目)來輔助教學。  \nThe 21st century is the era of biotechnology and big data. Do you know what is gene? What are relationships among DNA, RNA, and protein? How DNA play critical roles in whole life? What is genetically modified organism (GMO)? Students will learn an insight into genes from this course. On the other hand, biotechnology is an interdisciplinary science. The students will know why computer science, statistics, mathematics, physics, and chemistry are all required for revealing the genetic codes. Not only lectures, but also several related video will be performed in this class.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   21世紀是生物科技的時代，那麼你知道”基因”到底是甚麼嗎?\n*   本課程將利用自製講義讓學生了解基因是甚麼，以及其背後隱藏的秘密。\n*   學生透過本課程的學習能了解基因背後所蘊藏的意義，以及生物科技研究領域的多元化。\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介 |\n| 2 | 甚麼是DNA?基因在哪裡? |\n| 3 | 從DNA、RNA到蛋白質 (1) |\n| 4 | 從DNA、RNA到蛋白質 (2) |\n| 5 | PCR是甚麼?基因工程是甚麼?     "課程大綱": "Title: 從醫學看健康生活MEDICAL SCIENCE OF LIFE 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A92C500&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n□ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n「健康生活」? 看似很簡單的議題，網紅的專家也很多，但是不是常愈看愈不知所云？近幾年食安問題頻傳，到底要如何吃才是健康、安全？肥胖、三高、糖尿病、心血管疾病等，隨著人類的文明進展，愈來愈多的健康問題，讓大家焦慮、恐慌，都反應出要維持「不生病」的健康生活，現代人應該都要具備一些基本的常識，才能辨別真偽資訊、食得安心並生活得健康。 本課程從「醫學學理」的角度來談健康生活，以深入淺出的方式，從認識人體代謝有關的基本常識與觀念，逐步讓同學了解到生活飲食與健康維持間的關係，再進階到當健康出現問題，疾病是如何發生，特別舉肥胖、三高、癌症、糖尿病等常見的疾病，做進一步的介紹，讓同學具備正確的概念；此外，課程中也讓同學了解生活環境中，哪裡有細菌？也談談真的是「不乾不淨吃了沒病」嗎？網路上跟健康有關的迷思又該如何釐清？惱人的青春痘、外表看似不起眼的蜂窩性組織炎都跟細菌感染有關嗎？本課程也特別邀請感染專科醫師來介紹發燒就是有感染嗎、何時該用抗生素等議題，以建構同學基本的健康常識。 此外，由於知識是永遠學不完的，課堂同時也教導同學如何搜尋網路資訊，解答生活上的疑惑，並對於基改、農藥、有機等複雜議題應該具備哪些正確的認識，提供未來面臨個人健康、以及生活上飲食、藥物、預防醫學等方面問時的參考，並擴及到家人健康生活的應用，所以，只要帶著主動、好奇、長知識的心情進入課堂，相信學習可以是充實、愉快的。  \nHealthy life may seem to be a very simple topic. Experts and influencers are talking about it in every channel. But, is it becoming more and more inexplicable? Civilization apparently brings health problems such as obesity, three “hypers” (high blood pressure, blood sugar, and cholesterol), diabetes mellitus, cardiovascular diseases, etc. that make us anxious or even panic. Those illnesses reflect the necessity of maintaining a healthy life with commonsense in order to learn authentic information, eat at ease, then live in a healthy lifestyle. This course provides information based on medical science. Through those common knowledge and basic concepts related to human metabolism, students will gradually understand the relationship between daily life diet and health maintenance, then achieve the goal of being healthy. For example, students would know where the bacteria are in the living environments? Whether “you'll eat a peck of dirt before you die (不乾不淨吃了沒病)” is true or not? How to verify those health-related myths from content farms and how to find reliable information? Are annoying pimples and seemingly obscure cellulitis related to bacterial infections? Doctors who specializes in infectious disease will also give lectures, introducing topics like the meaning of fever: is that equal to getting an infection? When should I take antibiotics? Lecturers will help student build up the health knowledge. Most importantly, it is purported to provide students correct understanding of complex issues including GMO products, pesticides, and organic products. The learning scope would also extend to self-learning of diet, medicine, and preventive medicine. These units are known as cells. In our everyday observations, cells in the plants can absorb light and produce energy. Cells in the animals can make them move and think. The components in the cells take care of different functions that are essential for maintaining life and forming various kinds of creatures. Although most of the cells share similar structure and function, how do they behave differently and generate distinct characteristics? In this class, we will explore the world of cells and figure out the diversity of cells in plants and animals that we see every day. We will be amazed by the capability of these cells and appreciate more about ourselves and the world surrounding us! This is an EMI course.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   Understand the function of a cell and its components\n*   Compare the difference of the cells from plants and animals\n*   Explain the cell functions to the daily life events\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 傾聽與對話:冰山理論奇幻之旅THE CONVERSATION JOURNEY OF ICEBERG METAPHOR 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A92U100&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n■ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n■ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n□ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n■ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n□ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n冰山理論是家族治療先驅薩提爾女士提出來的隱喻，將個人的表層的應對行為與深層的渴望比喻成一座冰山，本課程以傾聽與對話的方式，高度互動討論與實作練習，學習薩提爾的冰山理論。培養傾聽、觀察、提問、探索生命歷程、尋找正向資源的能力。  \nThe iceberg theory is a metaphor model by Virginia Satir, a pioneer of family therapy, which describe a personal behaviors and deep desires like an iceberg. This course uses listening and dialogue, highly interactive discussions and practice to learn Satir's iceberg model. Develop the ability to listen, observe, ask questions, explore the life journey, and find positive resources.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   培養自我覺察的能力\n*   培養冰山理論的基礎概念\n*   培養跨域溝通與創意實作的能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 初探薩提爾的冰山理論 |\n| 2 | 設計奇幻旅程 |\n| 3 | 傾聽與陪伴練習 |\n| 4 | 敘事與提問練習 |\n| 5 | 大學生100種煩惱 |\n| 6 | 大學生100種資源 |\n| 7 | 大學生到此一遊(簡歷敘事) 準備一頁A4簡歷 |\n| 8 | 探索專家的成長旅程 英雄之旅學習單 |\n| 9 | 攝影創作I(觀察) 攝影實作 |\n| 10 | 攝影創作II(資料蒐集) 攝影實作 |\n| 11 | 手繪創作I(自由曲線)\\*觸覺治療(藝術感知探索、身體知覺) |\n| 12 | 手繪創作II(人的連結) |\n| 13 | 如何好奇生活環境\\*聽覺治療(生活環境聲響、電影中的聲音張力) |\n| 14 | 如何發現正向資源 |\n| 15 | 小組實作I(奇幻旅程規劃) 奇幻旅程構想書 \\*聽覺治療(聲音陪伴優化生命價值) |\n| 16 | 小組實作II(奇幻旅程體驗) 奇幻旅程迭代紀錄 |\n| 17 | 小組實作III(奇幻旅程反思) 奇幻旅程完整提案 |\n| 18 | 尋找冰山光廊裡的資源 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Sudden and severe cardiovascular dysfunction results in a threat to our life. However, our stressful life and unhealthy habit are the risk factors of cardiovascular diseases. Therefore, it is important for us to maintain daily healthcare and healthy life via understanding the cardiovascular homeostasis and the risk factors, clinical symptoms and medication of relevant cardiovascular diseases.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解健康狀態時的心血管運作\n*   分析疾病情境時的心血管異常\n*   釐清治療時的心血管反應\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程引言 |\n| 2 | 健康的心臟運作要件 |\n| 3 | 健康的血管系統運作要件 |\n| 4 | 健康的血液運作要件 |\n| 5 | 隱形殺手高血壓 |\n| 6 | 三分糖可以嗎? |\n| 7 | 作怪的荷爾蒙 |\n| 8 | 小心高血脂來敲門 |\n| 9 | 學習反思 |\n| 10 | 要命之心衰竭與冠狀動脈疾病 |\n| 11 | 心臟血管生死搏命一線間 |\n| 12 | 發炎四部曲:感染疾病雙面刃？ |\n| 13 | 肺部也有高血壓？ |\n| 14 | 高血壓腎病vs.腎性高血壓，傻傻分不清楚 |\n| 15 | 小鹿亂撞：談心律不整 |\n| 16 | 劣化的工作細胞 |\n| 17 | 學習反思 |\n| 18 | 課程回饋 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? How do they interfere with the body? This course is based on common cases of substance toxicity in life (hydrophobic oil, cadmium rice, lean meat, green oysters, plasticizers, Puffini eggs, etc., guide students to understand the basic characteristics of diet, home or environmental toxic substances, ways to enter the body, impact on the human body and major harmful effects, and then understand the basic concepts of toxicology, and learn and evaluate Affecting toxic pollution events in Taiwan\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   學習日常生活中常見毒性物質的常識\n*   體認日常生活中的常見毒物對於身體不同系統之影響\n*   了解外在環境中的毒化物及其作用機制\n*   認識環境中的毒化物對人體的影響\n*   分析生活中的毒物相關社會事件，提出看法及具備自我思辨的能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介 |\n| 2 | 「解」毒 |\n| 3 | 毒化物也會爆肝 Material selection methods is introduced such as material factors and performance indexes. Learn to use and draw material selection diagrams by yourself, and import a large number of design cases to illustrate the factors that need to be considered when selecting materials in practice, such as process, shape, combine material, multiple restrictions and conflicting goals. The course also mentions environmental factors and the importance of industrial design.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   材料的特性以及分析方法\n*   分析使用條件\n*   因應不同使用環境選擇適當材料\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Introduction: Materials and Design |\n| 2 | Engineering Materials and Their Properties |\n| 3 | Material Property Charts |\n| 4 | Materials Selection-The basic |\n| 5 | Materials Selection-The basic |\n| 6 | Materials Selection-Case studies 1 |\n| 7 | Materials Selection-Case studies 2 |\n| 8 | Materials Selection-Case studies 3 |\n| 9 | Materials Selection-Case studies 4 |\n| 10 | Processes and Their Effect on Properties |\n| 11 | Processes and Their Effect on Properties |\n| 12 | Processes Selection and Cost |\n| 13 | Processes Selection and Cost |\n| 14 | Multiple Constraints an Conflicting Objectives |\n| 15 | Multiple Constraints an Conflicting Objectives -Case Studies |\n| 16 | Conducting thin film |\n| 17 | Conducting thin film |\n| 18 | Final Exam |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 1 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 建築與抗震ARCHITECTURE AND EARTHQUAKE RESISTANCE 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A948600&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n□ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n台灣地處環太平洋地震帶，地震頻繁，災情頻傳，在地震災害中人命傷亡與財物損失之主要原因乃因建築結構物倒塌所致。因此，結構與耐震技術已成為土木建築專業領域中不可或缺之項目；然而，建築物乃民眾日常生活起居或外界活動空間之所在，因此建築地震防災常識可為台灣居民生活必要常識之一。本課程由地球科學領域中有關地球構造與板塊漂移之介紹引入地震成因與地震相關名詞解說，讓學生瞭解地震與震災報導中相關名詞之定義。由建築物構造類別與施工細則之差異瞭解生活中不同建築結構，諸如，鋼筋混凝土結構、鋼骨結構及木造結構物在地震時之反應。經由不同建築物平面結構型式與不同立面結構型式抗震行為及建築物之隔震結構措施之瞭解，可辨別居家生活中不同建築型式房屋之耐震與隔震能力。在居家抗震、海嘯防護與社區避難之課程內容中，將震災防護之標準操作程序融入日常生活中。最後討論目前國家所制訂之災害防治法及相關法規以及技術規範條文與目前施行之情況。本課程為跨理工及社會科學，管理科學領域之課程，課程內容可培養學生具有國際視野公民素養，並具有慎思明辨與創新之生活實踐能力。  \nTaiwan is located in the Pacific Rim earthquake zone, with frequent earthquakes and frequent disasters. The main causes of human casualties and property losses in earthquake disasters are caused by the collapse of building structures. Therefore, structure and earthquake-resistant technology have become indispensable items in the field of civil engineering; however, buildings are where people live and work or outside activities, so building earthquake disaster prevention common sense can be one of the necessary common sense for Taiwan residents. This course introduces the explanations of the causes of earthquakes and earthquake-related terms from the introduction of earth structure and plate drift in the field of earth science, so that students can understand the definitions of related terms in earthquake and earthquake reporting. Learn about the response of different building structures in life, such as reinforced concrete structures, steel skeleton structures, and wooden structures, from the differences in building construction categories and construction details. Through the understanding of the seismic behavior of different types of building plane structure types and different facade structure types and the seismic isolation structure measures of buildings, it is possible to distinguish the seismic resistance and isolation capabilities of different building types of houses in daily life. In the course content of home earthquake resistance, tsunami protection and community evacuation, standard operating procedures for earthquake disaster protection are integrated into daily life. Finally, we discuss the current disaster prevention laws, relevant regulations, and technical specifications and the current implementation situation. This course is a course that spans the fields of science and engineering, social sciences, and management science. The content of the course can cultivate students with an international vision of civic literacy, as well as the ability to think carefully and innovate in life.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   瞭解地震之成因與可能造成之災害\n*   認識房屋建築構造之類別\n*   瞭解建築耐震之基本原理\n*   居家地震防護\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 第01週：地球構造與板塊漂移學說 |\n| 2 | 第02週：地震的定義與成因 |\n| 3 | 第03週：斷層與台灣之活動斷層 |\n| 4 | 第04週：震源、震央、規模與震度 |\n| 5 | 第05週：地震災害 |\n| 6 | 第06週：建築構造類別與施工細則 |\n| 7 | 第07週：建築物之地震反應 |\n| 8 | 第08週：期中考試 |\n| 9 | 第09週：建築物結構之抗震 |\n| 10 | 第10週：建築物之隔震結構 |\n| 11 | 第11週：建築物耐震設計規範 |\n| 12 | 第12週：居家抗震 |\n| 13 | 第13週：災害防治法簡介 |\n| 14 | 第14週：地震相關法規 |\n| 15 | 第15週：課程調整 |\n| 16 | 第16週：期末考試 |\n| 17 | 第17週： |\n| 18 | 第18週： |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 應用化學與實驗FASCINATING CHEMISTRY AND EXPERIMENT 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A932002&class_code=1\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n□ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n□ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n課程包含化學原理解說與實驗操作。利用簡單的化學實驗操作，使同學瞭解化學的基本概念，教學內容偏向生活的應用化學原理與簡單易懂的實驗操作。主題的應用化學及相關實驗如下： 一 果凍蠟燭 目的：以簡單的器材及原料製作美觀之果凍蠟燭。 化學主題內涵：燃燒、物質變化、有機化合物、酸、醇、酯。 二 指紋的顯現 目的：利用物理或化學方法使隱藏的指紋顯現出來。 化學主題內涵：吸附、物理吸附、化學反應、氨基酸。三 鍊金術 目的：觀察銅幣經由銀色變成金色，以說明氧化還原反應。化學主題內涵：氧化、還原、氧化劑、還原劑、合金。 四 透明香皂 目的：將市售肥皂加工製成透明香皂。 化學主題內涵：肥皂、皂化反應、脂肪酸鹽、鹽析、透明香皂。 五 化學造影 目的：由鐵化合物化學反應產生的變化應用在紙張影像的顯現。 化學主題內涵：鐵、過渡金屬元素、配位化合物、光誘導還原反應。 六 酸鹼變色球 目的：利用紫色高麗菜中的色素製成球狀酸鹼指示劑，以此觀察在不同酸鹼性環境中其顏色之變化。 化學主題內涵：酸鹼值、酸鹼指示劑、聚合物、酸雨、環保。 七 彈性聚合物 目的：將聚乙烯醇和硼砂溶液混合製成透明的化學粘土。 化學主題內涵：高分子聚合物、單體、熱塑性塑膠、熱固性塑膠、塑膠回收。 八 閃爍的螢光 目的：了解螢光的產生及市售螢光棒的發光原理。 化學主題內涵：冷光、化學發光、魯米諾、過氧化物。九 銀鏡的製造 目的：利用氧化還原將銀離子還原至玻璃表面。 化學主題內涵：銀鏡反應、無電極電鍍、還原、化學還原鍍。 十 葉脈網標本 目的：利用強鹼性溶液的腐蝕特性製成葉脈網標本。 化學主題內涵：呼吸作用、光合作用、鹼腐蝕。 十一 感溫顯色薄膜 目的：利用具有液晶特性的化合物製成感溫液晶膜。 化學主題內涵：液晶分子、相變、異向性、旋光性。  \nThis course includes introduction of chemical principles and the corresponding experimental practices focused on applications of chemistry in everyday life. This course covers the following topics: 1-Jelly Candles: combustion, organic compounds; 2-Fingerprint Collection: adsorption, chemical reactions; 3- Gold Penny: redox reaction, alloy; 4-Transparent Soap: saponification, surfactant; 5-Cyanotype: coordination complex, light-induced reduction; 6-Colors of Anthocyanins: acid-base reaction, biological pigments; 7- Elastic Polymers: addition and condensation polymerizations; 8-Chemiluminescence: cold light, peroxides; 9-Silver Mirrors: electroless deposition; 10-Leaf Veins of Plant: caustic treatment; 11-Thermochromatic Films: liquid crystals.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   藉由與生活相結合的化學原理與實驗操作，將化學基本的概念普及於較少接觸化學的同學\n*   設計簡單易懂且有趣的實驗主題，使同學加深對化學原理的印象\n*   親自操作方式印證化學原理\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程概述 |\n| 2 | 實驗室安全講習 |\n| 3 | 指紋的顯現 |\n| 4 | 煉金術 |\n| 5 | 果凍蠟燭 |\n| 6 | 透明香皂 |\n| 7 | 化學造影 |\n| 8 | 研討 |\n| 9 | 研討 |\n| 10 | 期中考試 |\n| 11 | 酸鹼變色球 |\n| 12 | 彈性聚合物 |\n| 13 | 閃爍的螢光 |\n| 14 | 銀鏡的製造 |\n| 15 | 葉脈網標本 |\n| 16 | 感溫顯色薄膜(研討) |\n| 17 | 研討 |\n| 18 | 期末考試 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? How many times? No  \n2.本課程是否規劃含校外實習(並非參訪)? 否  \nAre there any internships involved in the course? How many hours? No  \n3.本課程是否可歸認為學術倫理課程? 否  \nIs this course recognized as an academic ethics course? In the course how many hours are regarding academic ethics topics? No  \n4.本課程是否屬進入社區實踐課程? 否  \nIs this course recognized as a Community engagement and Service learning course? Which community will be engaged? No\n"

    "課程大綱": "Title: 生活中玩光電PLAYING WITH LIGHT AND PHOTONICS 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A936800&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n□ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n課程包含光學/光電原理解說與實驗操作及團體討論。 以引導問題方式帶出要完成的實驗任務。透過學生的自主探索和團隊合作來解決問題，由簡單的實驗從而學習潛藏在問題背後的光電科學知識，進而養成解決問題的技能和自主學習的能力。實驗內容會生活中的光電應用為主。每學期預計完成6-7個光學/光電實驗，以兩周完成一個實驗的實作與科學探索討論。  \nBased on the experiments, the instructor will guide the students to solve the problem. The students take place independent observation and teamwork discussion to finish the task. According to several simple optics experiments, they will learn how to express their findings in daily life. Furthermore, students will develop problem-solving skills and self-learning abilities. The experimental content includes 6-7 optical/photonic experiments. Each experiment includes hand-on part and discussion within 4 hours.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   由生活中的光電現象啟發問題，團體討論後經由實驗瞭解各種日常生活中的光學光電現象\n*   從動手做中學習，培養學生觀察紀錄與科學探索分析的思辨與批判思考能力\n*   增進文學院、社科學院，管理學院以及規劃設計學院的學生跨域能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 講解課程與光電實驗安全注意事項 |\n| 2 | 光電科技介紹 |\n| 3 | 光的折射與成像:以簡易手機光學顯微鏡觀察微小物體 |\n| 4 | 講解、團體討論前週實驗與光電展演實驗 |\n| 5 | 全反射原理與光纖:利用愛玉及水來做全反射實驗 |\n| 6 | 講解、團體討論前週實驗與光電展演實驗 |\n| 7 | 光的偏振性:以偏振片觀察光源偏振現象（主要觀察液晶螢幕及反射光），與觀察應力現象（光彈效應） |\n| 8 | 講解、團體討論前週實驗與光電展演實驗 |\n| 9 | 自組光譜儀觀察LED、雷射、固態白光及各式光源特性實驗 (1) |\n| 10 | 自組光譜儀觀察LED、雷射、固態白光及各式光源特性實驗 (2) |\n| 11 | 講解、團體討論前週實驗與光電展演實驗 |\n| 12 | 認識數位光學 (I) : 組裝光學樂高積木與動手架光路 |\n| 13 | 認識數位光學 (II): 光調製器介紹與干涉繞射實驗 |\n| 14 | 認識數位光學 (III): 數位顯示技術 |\n| 15 | 講解、團體討論前週實驗、光電美的饗宴照片拍攝、綜合實驗 |\n| 16 | 團體報告 |\n| 17 | 自主學習與體驗生活中的光電現象 |\n| 18 | 自主學習與體驗生活中的光電應用 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? It adopts the \"Double Diamond\" thinking model, a human-centered innovation approach that emphasizes creating value by deeply understanding user needs and challenges. The framework for solving complex problems is divided into two stages: problem understanding and problem-solving. By combining these methods, the course employs design thinking to gain insights into problems and then explores and experiments with solutions within the Double Diamond model. This combination ensures that solutions meet user needs and are innovative. By bringing together faculty, students, and professionals from various fields, the course aims to redefine industry problems, collaborate on co-creation research platforms, and teach students about semiconductor industry trends, equipment operation, and maintenance. Through real-world case studies, students apply the methods they have learned to solve practical problems. This integrated teaching model not only bridges the gap between theory and practice but also provides students with industry-oriented training, thereby promoting innovation and talent development in the semiconductor industry.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? The course will guide students to understand the design and application of integrated circuits. They will mainly learn the principles of integrated circuits, system design methods, related applications, international trends and market development. Over the years, earthquakes have caused building collapses and frequent casualties. This course provides knowledge of earthquake resistance, seismic isolation, and energy dissipation system for non-civil engineering and architecture students through online teaching videos, scale-down teaching aids and teaching plans developed by this lecture. Users can understand the theory and complete simple experiments. Through experimental observation, recording and adjustment of variable factors, the goal of multiple learning is achieved. In addition, this course also introduces the preliminary assessment system of earthquake resistance, and promotes the knowledge of disaster prevention, mitigation and relief.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解房地產發展趨勢與購屋需求\n*   認識建築結構與耐震安全議題\n*   結合專業系所學科知識發展耐震安全技術\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介 |\n| 2 | 房價高漲好房難尋？ |\n| 3 | 我應該買房嗎？ |\n| 4 | 耐震級數有幾g？ |\n| 5 | RC/SS/SRC誰耐震？ |\n| 6 | 格局方正好在哪？ |\n| 7 | 柱梁版牆在哪裡？ |\n| 8 | 嚇，房子震倒了？ |\n| 9 | 台北城裝在布丁盒？ |\n| 10 | 土壤變液體？ |\n| 11 | 地基挖呀挖呀挖？ |\n| 12 | 孔固力要幾磅？ |\n| 13 | 無敵鐵筋鋼？ |\n| 14 | 耐震要標章？ |\n| 15 | 隔震沒感覺？ |\n| 16 | 減震減幾趴？ |\n| 17 | 評估補強救命符？ |\n| 18 | 優質建商求推薦？ |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   就業與經濟成長 (Decent work and Economic growth)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 科技與國防INTRODUCTION TO NEW TECHNOLOGY AND NATIONAL DEFENCE 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A933002&class_code=1\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n本課程以分析國防科技產業發展模式，增進學生科研知識及解決問題能力，最終則希望培養學生獨立學習與團隊合作精神 ，成為高科技專業人才。課程內容設計如下： 緒言 第1章 現代科技與戰爭發展 第2章 現代科技與武器發展 第3章 高科技資訊武器 第4章 美國前瞻國防產業與任務解決介紹 第5章 前瞻科技與國防之十大標竿成果簡介 第6章 前瞻科技與企業間之互動機制 第7章 我國國防前瞻科技及研發現況介紹 第8章 前瞻科技與國防之未來轉型趨勢 第9章 前瞻科研武器發展現況及對未來戰爭影響 小組報告  \nThe course analyzes the industry development model of the national defense science and technology in order to increase students' research knowledge and problem solving ability. Finally, this course aims to enhance learning autonomy and the cooperataion spirit of the students, helping them become high-tech professionals. The course is designed as follows : Introduction Chapter 1 Modern technology and the development of war. Chapter 2 Modern technology and the development of weapons. Chapter 3 High-tech information weapons. Chapter 4 The introduction of USA new national defense industry and the mission resolution. Chapter 5 Introduction to the results of top ten R&D Program of new technology and national defense. Chapter 6 The interaction mechanism between new technology and industrial enterprises. Chapter 7 Introduction of R&D situation and new technology of the national defense in ROC. Chapter 8 The future transformation trend of new technology and national defense. Chapter 9 New technology weapons development and the effects to the future war. Chapter 7 Introduction of R&D situation and new technology of the national defense in ROC. Chapter 8 The future transformation trend of new technology and national defense. Chapter 9 New technology weapons development and the effects to the future war.     "課程大綱": "Title: 虛擬世界之設計與研究VIRTUAL WORLD DESIGN AND RESEARCH 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A94E900&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n■ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n□ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n虛擬世界是數位化的互動或模擬環境。隨著社會需求的變化和科技的進步，「虛擬」和「實體」世界之間的界線和相互依賴關係也持續變化。本課程介紹了虛擬世界設計的理論和實踐，以及互動環境中的研究主題。通過講課、實際設計專案、和研究作業的結合，學生將學習創作虛擬世界的原則，檢視與虛擬空間研究相關的社會議題，並探討相關主題在各個領域中的應用。  \nVirtual worlds are digitally interactive or simulated environments. With varying societal needs and technological advancement, the boundary and dependence between “virtual” and “physical” worlds constantly change. The course introduces the theories and practices of designing virtual worlds, along with research topics in interactive digital environments. With a combination of lectures, hands-on design projects, and research assignments, students will learn the principles of virtual world creation, examine the societal considerations of research in virtual spaces, and explore applications in various fields.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   Understand the principles and theories of virtual world design.\n*   Conceptualize and design virtual environments.\n*   Develop plans for conducting research in virtual worlds.\n*   Creatively and substantially generate, present, and comment on course projects.\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Course Overview |\n| 2 | History and Basic Concepts of Virtual Worlds |\n| 3 | Virtual Reality, Augmented Reality, and Mixed Reality |\n| 4 | Reality, Presence, and Immersion |\n| 5 | Multimodal Interactions for XR |\n| 6 | Tutorial: Virtual World Creation (1) |\n| 7 | Collaboration and Communities (in Physical and Virtual Worlds) |\n| 8 | MMPRPGs |\n| 9 | Interaction Design Principles for Virtual Worlds |\n| 10 | Project 1: Submission/Presentation |\n| 11 | Avatars and Identity: Uncanny Valley |\n| 12 | Avatars and Identity: Proteus Effect |\n| 13 | Tutorial: Virtual World Creation (2) |\n| 14 | Simulation and Digital Twins (1) |\n| 15 | Simulation and Digital Twins (2) |\n| 16 | Game Design, Game Mechanics, and Gamification |\n| 17 | Project 2: Submission/Presentation |\n| 18 | Discussion and Reflection |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course     "課程大綱": "Title: 醫療與文化MEDICINE & CULTURE 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A92N700&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n本課程探討影響各種文化中醫療的異同，以及會影響醫療和與健康相關的信念及實踐的各種社會力量。本課程的目的是使學生熟悉醫學信仰和實踐的比較性，跨文化研究，包括醫學人類學中有關健康和疾病的關鍵研究，概念和方法。  \nThis course explores the similarities and differences in health care across cultures and the social forces that affect health and health-related beliefs and practices. The goal of the course is to familiarize students with the comparative, cross-cultural study of medical beliefs and practices, including key research, concepts, and approaches to health and illness in medical anthropology.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   Understand differences in health approaches worldwide in cultural context.\n*   Analyze ethnomedical systems through cross-cultural comparison.\n*   Communicate better with people from different cultures about health issues.\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Course Introduction: Course Theme, Grading, Medical Anthropology, Key concepts |\n| 2 | Course Introduction (cont.): Cultural Constructs, Well-being, Illness & Suffering, Ritual Process, Metaphor |\n| 3 | What’s so medical about disease? (Fieldwork Example: Peruvian Shaman)(read Joralemon) |\n| 4 | Local Meanings of“Global Biomedicine”全球生物醫學的在地意義Part I—Cultural Differences within Biomedicine; Medical Pluralism; Integrative Medicine; Example around the World |\n| 5 | Local Meanings of“Global Biomedicine”全球生物醫學的在地意義: Part II—Biomedicine as an Ethnomedicine: Comparing Germany, U.S., France, U.K., & Taiwan (read Payer) |\n| 6 | Placebo Response/Meaning Effect安慰劑反應/意義效應: Social Theories; Examples; If Patient’s Aware; Role in RCTs; as Core Metaphor of Biomedical Unknowns (read Resnick) |\n| 7 | Cultural Expressions of Distress: Epidemic Trance Possession among Children in Suriname (South America) & eSwatini (formerly Swaziland, southern Africa) 苦難文化表現形式: 蘇里南共和國和史瓦帝尼王國兒童的精神恍惚流行病 (read Reis) |\n| 8 | Epidemic Trance Possession in Southeast Asia |\n| 9 | Culture-bound Syndromes文化特有症候群 (Example: AIDS Neurosis in Japan)(read Miller) |\n| 10 | Student Presentations on Culture-Bound Syndromes around the World |\n| 11 | Student Presentations on Culture-Bound Syndromes around the World (continued) |\n| 12 | Shamanism Ancient & Modern古代與現代的巫師 (read Brown) |\n| 13 | Watch Documentary Film, “The Last Shaman” (0.5 page essay on film due next week) |\n| 14 | Shamanism, Christianity, and Tourism in a Tsou Village in Taiwan |\n| 15 | Quiz 1: Shamans & Shamanism. Period 2: Discussion of quiz & “The Last Shaman” Film. Students doing Final Research Project: Meet with Teacher. |\n| 16 | Quiz 2: Ethnomedicines, Placebo; Cultural Expressions of Distress; Culture-Bound Syndromes. Period 2: Discussion in class of the quiz. Students doing Final Research Project: Meet with Teacher. |\n| 17 | Supplement Marketing in Taiwan; Marketing Health Products - Supplements, Medicine Shows & Popular Media保健產品的行銷：補給品，醫學展演和大眾媒體 |\n| 18 | Understanding Bioscience Lab Research as a Cultural Practice: Spirituality in Taiwan (read Thomas; De Cruz; Lambek) |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   性別平等 (Gender Equality)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Introduce existing intelligent care technologies, such as wearable devices, decision support systems, virtual health assistants, etc. Discuss how intelligent care can be applied in the field of mental health, such as monitoring patient behavior patterns, emotional states, etc., to provide real-time information and intervention. Understand the ethical and legal issues of using intelligent care technology in mental health, such as patient privacy rights, data security, etc.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解精神健康的定義及內涵\n*   認識常見精神疾病及治療\n*   認識現有智慧照護技術\n*   了解及分析智慧照護於精神健康相關倫理與法律議題\n*   探討智慧照護如何應用於精神健康領域，並構思可行的精神健康智慧照護實作方案\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介 |\n| 2 | 精神健康的定義及內涵 |\n| 3 | 精神健康風險及精神疾病 |\n| 4 | 常見精神疾病及治療 |\n| 5 | 精神健康之自我照護 |\n| 6 | 小組實作活動 (I) |\n| 7 | 智慧照護概念 |\n| 8 | 智慧照護技術 |\n| 9 | 智慧照護於健康領域之應用 |\n| 10 | 小組實作活動 (II) |\n| 11 | 智慧照護於精神健康領域之應用 |\n| 12 | 期中考 |\n| 13 | 小組實作活動 (III) |\n| 14 | 智慧照護於精神健康之倫理與法律議題 |\n| 15 | 小組實作成果展 (I) |\n| 16 | 小組實作成果展 (II) |\n| 17 | 小組實作成果展 (III) |\n| 18 | 期末評值 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n*   全球夥伴 (Partnerships for goals)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Thus, design thinking is a form of solution-focused thinking which starts with a goal (a better future situation) instead of solving one specific problem. In this course, we will lead students to learn DT practice and apply to creativity, innovation, and entrepreneurship. Design thinking is an iterative problem solving process of discovery, ideation, and experimentation that employs design based techniques to gain insight and yield innovative solutions for virtually any type of organizational or business challenge, prominently including those within public service. In this course, we will unpack each step of the design thinking process and become familiar with the design thinker's toolkit. Over the course, students will directly apply what they have learned to cultural and creative industries, public service and social entrepreneurial challenges about which they are passionate: they will untangle the complexities of related policy and explore innovative ways to create real impact.  \nThe goal of Design Thinking is matching people’s needs with what is technologically feasible and viable as a business strategy\" Students expect to learn by knowing about how designers approach problems and the methods which they use to ideate, select and execute solutions, individuals and businesses will be better able to improve their own problem solving processes and take innovation to a higher level. Thus, design thinking is a form of solution-focused thinking which starts with a goal (a better future situation) instead of solving one specific problem. In this course, we will lead students to learn DT practice and apply to creativity, innovation, and entrepreneurship. Design thinking is an iterative problem solving process of discovery, ideation, and experimentation that employs design based techniques to gain insight and yield innovative solutions for virtually any type of organizational or business challenge, prominently including those within public service. In this course, we will unpack each step of the design thinking process and become familiar with the design thinker's toolkit. Over the course, students will directly apply what they have learned to cultural and creative industries, public service and social entrepreneurial challenges about which they are passionate: they will untangle the complexities of related policy and explore innovative ways to create real impact.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   學習創意、創新、創業的相關知識與精神\n*   瞭解創意發想與創新思考的脈絡並能操作與運用\n*   讓非設計領域的學生了解設計思維的基本概念與精神\n*   瞭解創意創新到創業之間的差異與關連性\n*   了解不同專業領域與創新之間的連結與發展\n*   能習得跨領域團隊合作的經驗與能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程及評分方式概述 |\n| 2 | 中秋節放假 |\n| 3 | 從創意創新到創業之關聯性與個案分享 |\n| 4 | 創意創新與設計思維 - 設計思維概論 |\n| 5 | 智慧財產權與三創 |\n| 6 | 從創意創新到創業落地I -概述與關聯 |\n| 7 | 從創意創新到創業落地II -如何培養? 如何有系統地進行? |\n| 8 | 從創意創新到創業落地III -個案討論 |\n| 9 | 創意引導 1：如何讓自己與別人都有創意 |\n| 10 | 創意引導 2：如何運用多種方法激發創意 |\n| 11 | 創意引導 3：如何針對特定問題執行創意 |\n| 12 | 從空間談創新 |\n| 13 | 系列講座 - 性別影響力與創新 I |\n| 14 | 系列講座 - 性別影響力與創新 II |\n| 15 | 系列講座 - 性別影響力與創新 III |\n| 16 | 團體期末報告 |\n| 17 | 團體期末報告 |\n| 18 | 期末考周 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Students will know the importance of the builting up the barrier-free environment and outdoor activities will be safer and more convenient for those disabled. The course is combined with service learning, providing the opportunities for students to experience the assistant devices and think about the appropriateness of barrier-free facilities in public environment. Where are the barrier-free facilities? Is it convenience for disabled users? How to use these facilities safely and correctly? What kind of facilities should be added to assist the disabled users? Does the design of these facilities truly meet the needs of the disabled? Is there anything to improve? The course will also guide the students how to integrate information with technology, to practice the manufacture of mobile application, experience the integration of medical professional and information technology.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   輔具之正確使用方式、無障礙空間規定\n*   體驗校園內無障礙空間設計及規劃\n*   以AR開發台南古蹟觀光景點內的無障礙設施和服務介紹\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介-有愛無障 |\n| 2 | 有愛無障 - 認識身心障礙者 |\n| 3 | 金剛芭比林欣蓓演講 - 我的限制級人生 |\n| 4 | 生活無障礙 - 食、住 |\n| 5 | 10/10(放假) |\n| 6 | 生活無障礙 - 行、育、樂 |\n| 7 | 無障礙設施設計規範 |\n| 8 | 無障礙硬體設施於國內外之應用 |\n| 9 | 無障礙軟體設計於國內外之應用 |\n| 10 | 議題探索 |\n| 11 | 室內無障礙行動模式：輔具資源中心 |\n| 12 | 各式行動輔具及使用方式/使用輔具於校園內行動 |\n| 13 | 無障礙設施調查建置AR方法 |\n| 14 | 台南知名古蹟無障礙環境探查(1) |\n| 15 | 台南知名古蹟無障礙環境探查(2) |\n| 16 | 古蹟無障礙環境AR製作(1) |\n| 17 | 古蹟無障礙環境AR製作(2) |\n| 18 | 期末分享-反思、成果與成長期末報告：規劃設計的AR(簡報、服務學習影片上傳)期末服務心得報告繳交 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? In the face of rapid social changes, this course will explore the social needs and domain knowledge of healthy living in different stages of modern high-age society, and explore ways and wisdom to promote healthy living from the six aspects of food, clothing, housing, travel, education and music. The application, and through the group discussion and practical application design thinking, proposes the problem situation and design plan for the healthy life of the elderly.\n\n課程學習目標 Course The course provides a general introduction of biomedical engineering by going thru fundamental and advance topics in biomedical engineering. The covered fields include: biomechanics, biomaterial, bioelectronics, rehabilitation engineering, bioimage, biosensor and medical care.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   An ability to apply knowledge of mathematics, science, and engineering.\n*   An understanding of professional and ethical responsibility\n*   To provides a general introduction of biomedical engineering\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程說明 |\n| 2 | 周鼎贏老師 |\n| 3 | 電腦視覺 |\n| 4 | 吳炳慶老師 |\n| 5 | 生醫用工程力學 |\n| 6 | 楊閎蔚老師 |\n| 7 | 嵌入式人工智慧運算及生成式人工智慧在醫療的應用 |\n| 8 | 準備期中考 |\n| 9 | 生醫工程學在骨科臨床之應用 |\n| 10 | 楊子賢老師 |\n| 11 | 超音波之生醫應用 |\n| 12 | 舒宇宸老師 |\n| 13 | 微細胞晶片裝置 |\n| 14 | 葉明龍老師 |\n| 15 | 鄭國順老師 |\n| 16 | 課後輔導 |\n| 17 | 課後輔導 |\n| 18 | 期末考週 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 藝術媒介與人權HUMAN RIGHTS THROUGH ARTS 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A93D900&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n■ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n■ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n■ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n爭取人權經常伴隨著社會上的創傷記憶，透過自傳、口述歷史、紀錄片可以保存歷史，透過文學、紀錄片、戲劇等藝術媒介的再現能讓許多個人的經驗拓展其影響範圍成為社會思考的議題。本課程分為性別平權、醫療平權及移工議題等多方面探討如何透過藝術媒介展現人權議題，透過台灣及國際人權藝術作品的分析幫助學生了解歷史並且能進一步參與詮釋並關注人權議題。  \nThe pursuit of human rights usually comes with the traumatic memory of society as the cost. To preserve history, autobiographies, oral history, and documentary films are all common and effective ways. Through literature, documentary films, plays, and other forms of art, personal experiences can be extended to make a greater impact on the society and generate discussion of certain issues. This course aims to examine how different forms of art serve as a medium to address human rights issues in three aspects: gender equality, healthcare equity, and migrant workers. By analyzing human rights-related artworks in Taiwan and other countries, this course can help students understand history and further interpret and shed light on human rights issues.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   透過臺灣社會運動中的創作來回顧與呈現不同時空下人權議題與藝術媒介的關係\n*   彰顯具備人權精神之藝術作品中所蘊含的特殊意義與藝術價值\n*   解析如何透過「文化介入」處理過去的社會抗爭、政治暴力與創傷記憶\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程說明 |\n| 2 | 劉振祥：人權運動的街頭風景 |\n| 3 | 紀錄劇場《1977聽見台灣之音》 |\n| 4 | 戲劇演出:《開在壁上的花》/海島演劇 |\n| 5 | 台南人權藝術節書展開幕講座 |\n| 6 | 羅士哲：「唸歌來相識，愈唸愈有力」 |\n| 7 | 黃勻弦：《山川壯麗》了嗎?影像創作的社會觀察與作用 |\n| 8 | 陳南宏：律政劇－在虛構的情節中呈現的真實社會 |\n| 9 | 沈邑蓎：在自己的衝突故事中找到裂縫-酷凌計畫 |\n| 10 | 校慶放假 |\n| 11 | 劉吉雄：作為「通道」的澎湖難民營 |\n| 12 | 尤哈尼‧伊斯卡卡夫特：母語是原住民族群的身分證 |\n| 13 | 周清玉：咱彰化－母語的歌與鄉土紮根運動 |\n| 14 | 陳柏偉：我們一起唱歌/黑手那卡西與社會運動 |\n| 15 | 藝術媒介與台灣的社會記憶 |\n| 16 | 演出觀摩 |\n| 17 | 演出觀摩 |\n| 18 | 綜合討論 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   性別平等 (Gender Equality)\n*   和平與正義制度 (Peace justice and strong institutions)\n*   全球夥伴 (Partnerships for goals)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 9 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? In total, 15 local and foreign teachers accompanied 160 local and foreign students in 12 library buses containing library books on 12 distinct topics (including reading, climate change and adaptation, and plant technology for sustainable agriculture) to engage in service-learning in 12 administrative districts across Tainan City.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n* The course assists students in drawing up plans at the beginning of the semester. Then students will carry out the project and do a presentation at the end of the semester. Under the guidance of one of the instructors from the teaching team, a student may form his or her project in the field of \"Society, Technology, and Medicine.\" The topics include health inequality, medical history, engineering history, and science communication. The project may be a research plan, an action plan, a short video or any project that is doable and approved by your instructor. It is preferable that students have taken one of the courses from the STM program previously (or during the same semester), and students are encouraged to develop their ideas through courses and receive guidance from a prior or concurrent STM course's teacher. If a student does not have any plan, he or she may choose a project from one ON the teachers’ list.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解科技與社會研究基礎研究方法\n*   整合不同領域知識\n*   應用研究方法解決實際問題\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程及授課團隊專長介紹 (教室) |\n| 2 | 研究的起點：研究案例 (教室) |\n| 3 | 研究的起點：研究案例 (教室) |\n| 4 | 何謂問題意識？何謂研究問題？ |\n| 5 | 研究法：檔案、訪談法(口述歷史) (教室)問卷設計及分析(教室) |\n| 6 | 研究案例/研究法：文獻分析(教室) |\n| 7 | 研究法：焦點團體訪談(教室) |\n| 8 | 研究法：田野調查(教室) |\n| 9 | 構想報告(1) (教室) |\n| 10 | 構想報告(2) (教室) |\n| 11 | 找老師討論構想 |\n| 12 | 找老師討論構想 |\n| 13 | 計畫方案實作 |\n| 14 | 進度報告 (到教室) |\n| 15 | 計畫方案實作 |\n| 16 | 計畫方案實作 |\n| 17 | 成果發表I (教室) |\n| 18 | 成果發表II (教室) |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? The first part focuses on emotional education, online-dating, intimate relationships from a gender equity perspective. The second part delves into the unfinished gender revolution that involving household division of labor, gender norms, and self-expectations. Through these materials, we help students understand the profound impact of patriarchal structures. Giving the social changes, this course also incorporates discussions on men’s studies and gender issues in AI.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Teaching strategies in the course include problem-based learning to enhance the awareness of globalization and its conflicts, collaborative learning to complete a group project, and service learning to enhance ethical thinking and the skills of problem-solving\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   跨域理解，發覺斜槓人生之美\n*   人文關懷，闡揚原民族群特色\n*   數位健康，培育數位照護行動\n*   放眼未來，以服務學習發展職涯\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹 |\n| 2 | 從包容科技談數位照護 |\n| 3 | 原民健康 |\n| 4 | 小組教學-自我偵測與練習 |\n| 5 | 社區活動規劃 |\n| 6 | 彈性課程 |\n| 7 | 文化敏感度 |\n| 8 | 文化踏查(來義) |\n| 9 | 彈性課程 |\n| 10 | 彈性課程 |\n| 11 | 彈性課程 |\n| 12 | 彈性課程 |\n| 13 | 彈性課程 |\n| 14 | 從探索中理解原民文化 |\n| 15 | 從探索中理解原民文化 |\n| 16 | 設計發展適合原鄉之數位照護 |\n| 17 | 設計發展適合原鄉之數位照護 |\n| 18 | 期末報告 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   淨水與衛生 (Clean water and sanitation)\n*   全球夥伴 (Partnerships for goals)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? First of all, it is necessary to analyze how to use modern technology products to bring about physical and mental health. For example, choose a safe and organic diet, reduce the use of plastic products to protect the ecology and environment of the earth. Students should learn to set high goals and start to treat people, appreciate the merits of others, learn to repay the kindness of others, and bring a good cycle to their interpersonal relationships in order to fully realize the value of life.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   瞭解科技帶來的利益和禍患，正確地使用科技。\n*   認清科技對環境的影響，如何改變自己的生活習慣。\n*   學習如何轉換角度看事情，遠離痛苦、邁向幸福。\n*   為自己的生命創造意義與價值，真實的面對自己的生命。\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description | 面授時數 | 同步時數 | 非同步時數 |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹 | 2 |  |  |\n| 2 | 科技與生命價值 |  |  | 2 |\n| 3 | 課程介紹 | 2 |  |  |\n| 4 | 大歷史，科技與生命價值 |  |  | 2 |\n| 5 | 感恩的力量 |  |  | 2 |\n| 6 | 物質與心靈的關係 |  |  | 2 |\n| 7 | 心靈的力量 |  |  | 2 |\n| 8 | 長遠的生命規劃 |  |  | 2 |\n| 9 | 科技人生的幸福與苦痛 |  |  | 2 |\n| 10 | 網路與人際關係 |  |  | 2 |\n| 11 | 21世紀的生命長度 |  |  | 2 |\n| 12 | 分組及小組討論 | 2 |  |  |\n| 13 | 小組討論 | 2 |  |  |\n| 14 | 小組討論 | 2 |  |  |\n| 15 | 期末報告 | 2 |  |  |\n| 16 | 簡報學 |  |  | 2 |\n| 17 | 簡報學 |  |  | 2 |\n| 18 | 簡報學 |  |  | 2 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n*   氣候行動 (Climate action)\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?
