However the economic impact generated by the outcomes of these researches is limited. The main reason is that these research outcomes are not well translated into business that may meet needs of the industry. Thus, how to well commercialize technology is a very important issue. In the course, the evaluation mechanisms of biotechnology commercialization will be introduced in terms of aspects of technology, regulations, patents, and finance. Also the real cases will be introduced to the students, which enables them to better understand the process of evaluation of commercialization and helps them make more feasible decision to accelerate commercial applications of technology. In the end, the goal of the course is expected to cultivate the students who possess knowledge and skills on integration of diverse disciplines and innovation.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   讓學生對於生技研發成果商品化的過程具備通識知識\n*   了解研發成果商業化評估，進而訂出可行的商業化策略，加速成果的商業應用\n*   期望培養學生跨領域整合與創新的知識與能力\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   健康與福祉 (Good health and Well Being)\n*   就業與經濟成長 (Decent work and Economic growth)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 1 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 資訊科技下的信任溝通之轉移THE TRANSFORMATION OF TRUST COMMUNICATION BY INFORMATION TECHNOLOGY 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A93D700&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n■ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n隨著新興科技數位轉型與零接觸科技發展的運用，遠距與線上應用、電子商務等經濟蓬勃發展，已成為人生活一部分，也影響人際信任與溝通方式。「零信任」(Zero Trust)此名詞概念，則是2010年首先由John Kindervag在擔任Forrester Research副總裁兼首席分析師時提出，其概念認為組織內部網路已基於各種安全設備保護(如防火牆等)下，是可受信任的，成為維持網路族群間相互交流過程之關鍵。此課程以零信任模型為主，探討科技安全與信任溝通行為對人類生活所產生之影響力。課程分為二大部分：第一部份說明科技「零信任」和「溝通」之意義，以及與管理信任之關係；第二部份，零信任的實踐實務性探討，即是瞭解零信任網路現在/未來發展動向，如科技與零信任的網路溝通行為對社會發展影響，如新創企業、網路媒體等問題。此課程將協助學生瞭解「科技」與「零信任」對網路安全溝通之重要性，故課程設計以重視零信任互動關係與科技行為之通則學習，期待各學系學生能有興趣學習。  \nWith the digital transformation, the applications of zero-touch technology, long-distance and online have flourished, which have become part of people's lives, and also affect interpersonal trust and communication methods. The term \"Zero Trust\" was first proposed by John Kindervag in 2010 when he was the vice president and chief analyst of Forrester Research. It becomes the key to maintaining the process of mutual communication on online groups. This course focuses on the zero-trust model, and explores the impact of technology security and trust communication behavior on human life. The course is divided into two parts: the first part explains the meaning of \"zero trust\" and \"communication\" in technology, and the relationship with managing trust; the second part, the practical discussion of zero trust in IT security, that is, understanding the zero trust network at the Current/future development trends through the impact of technology and zero-trust online communication behavior on social development, such as new startups, online media and other issues. This course will help students understand the importance of \"technology\" and \"zero trust\" to network security communication. Therefore, the course design emphasizes the general principles of zero-trust interaction and technology behavior. It is expected that students from various departments will be interested in learning trust.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   隨著科技數位轉型發展的運用，遠距與線上應用等蓬勃發展，已成為影響人際溝通方式。\n*   課程探討科技安全與信任溝通行為對人類生活所產生之影響力。\n*   協助學生瞭解「科技」與「信任」對網路安全溝通之重要性，以及人與科技運用責任承擔。\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 第一週 課程介紹-「科技信任」在哪裡? 「信任關係」是什麼？ |\n| 2 | 第二週 中秋節放假 |\n| 3 | 第三週 何謂「零信任」(Zero Trust)?與科技有何關係？「信任溝通」如何形成? --鄭志凱(2018)。信任，是溝通的母語。天下雜誌644期。(課堂討論) |\n| 4 | 第四週 科技與信任溝通之威脅型態演變 --2020 IEK零信任網路定義資通安全新觀念，IEKConsulting，頁1-10。 (繳交小組閱讀與討論作業) |\n| 5 | 第五週 自動化與零信任網路 --古涵詩(2022)，美國零信任安全應用與國際大廠動態，IEKConsulting，頁14-20。(課堂討論) |\n| 6 | 第六週 科技與管理信任溝通關係 --黃曼君(2021)，搶攻智慧城市商機的挑戰-社會對科技的信任風險，IEKConsulting，頁1-10。(繳交小組閱讀與討論作業) |\n| 7 | 第七週 對科技設備的信任 --蔡依寧(2017)。全球性組織之個人數據保護策略，IEKConsulting，頁1-11。 (課堂討論) |\n| 8 | 第八週 個案分析 --葉逸萱(2021)。2021 IEK\\_不可不知的元宇宙熱潮，IEKConsulting，頁1-10。 (繳交小組閱讀與討論作業) |\n| 9 | 第九週 11/05(二) 期中考 |\n| 10 | 第十週 對科技使用者的信任溝通 --池煥德等(2010)。數位科技在心理健康領域之發展分析，IEKConsulting，頁1-11。 (課堂討論) |\n| 11 | 第十一週 科技與國際趨勢 張峻菁(2024)。國際經驗助力台灣，賴政府「國家希望工程」之全球趨勢接軌策略研析，IEKConsulting，頁1-10。(繳交小組閱讀與討論作業) |\n| 12 | 第十二週 科技如何跨越信任溝通障礙？ --石育賢(2018)。全球自駕車如何跨越死亡之谷？IEKConsulting，頁1-10。(課堂討論) |\n| 13 | 第十三週 從「可解釋AI」到「可信任AI」 --陳右怡(2018)。全面解析:從｢可解釋 AI｣到｢可信任 AI｣，IEKConsulting，頁1-11。(繳交小組閱讀與討論作業) |\n| 14 | 第十四週 科技與信任溝通是自主或是依賴? These disasters including typhoon, earthquake, landslide and so on cost several economic and life losses. New technologies and management approaches have been adopted to reduce the damages and to enhance the disaster resilience. This program will introduce these new knowledge base on the aspects of engineering technology, design planning and management.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   建立學生對防災科技管理學分學程之整體概念\n*   使學生具備災害防救科技相關領域之基本知識\n*   使學生了解災害防救相關的科技與管理知識\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹 |\n| 2 | 國定假日 |\n| 3 | 斷層活動潛勢評估 |\n| 4 | 建築防火及逃生避難設計概論 |\n| 5 | 氣象災害及其防救科技 |\n| 6 | 洪旱災害及其防救科技  |\n| 7 | 橋梁耐震工程 |\n| 8 | 建築震損與耐震科技 |\n| 9 | 建築及文化資產防災規劃 |\n| 10 | 都市防災概論 |\n| 11 | 生存困境 |\n| 12 | 國土及區域規劃與防災 |\n| 13 | 災害防救體系及運作 |\n| 14 | 地震危害度評估概述 |\n| 15 | 災害認知與防災意識 |\n| 16 | 建築設備震損與耐震技術 |\n| 17 | 5D智慧城市防救災平台 |\n| 18 | 課程總結 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n*   永續城市與社區 (sustainable cities and communities)\n*   氣候行動 (Climate action)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Through the introduction to the basic geology related to the location of continents, the participants will understand how these magnific and unique lanscapes were formed and further learn how to appreciate the details of their beauty. In parallel, the history, cultural traditions and customs of various countries will be shared through the lecturer’s travel experiences. The participants are anticipated to learn the practical travel tips and to organize their own trips.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   從地質學角度認識世界\n*   擴大國際視野\n*   認識旅行的意義\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Introduction：旅行的意義 |\n| 2 | 旅行規劃 |\n| 3 | 旅行規劃 |\n| 4 | 冰與火之歌：冰島 |\n| 5 | 冰與火之歌：冰島 |\n| 6 | 世界末日？黃石國家公園超級火山 |\n| 7 | 地殼的創傷：夏威夷 |\n| 8 | 旅行計畫提案（分組報告） |\n| 9 | 世界之巔：喜馬拉雅山 |\n| 10 | 歐洲地質與文化概論 |\n| 11 | 歐洲地質與文化概論 |\n| 12 | 切、格瓦拉的摩托車日記：拉丁美洲 |\n| 13 | 太平洋火環：日本 |\n| 14 | 太平洋火環：台灣 |\n| 15 | 從地質學角度認識台灣 |\n| 16 | 分組報告 |\n| 17 | 分組報告 |\n| 18 | 分組報告 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course?     "課程大綱": "Title: 行動數位文化資產MOBILE DIGITAL CULTURE HERITAGE (M-DCH) 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A92S100&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n■ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n■ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n□ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n□ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n□ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n本課程的主題是結合IT技術與文化資產的行動數位文化資產（M-DCH）。與強調利用2/3D動畫技術進行虛擬文化資產探索的數位文化資產（DCH）不同，M-DCH強調的是攜帶手持裝置走進文化資產場域，進行無線-行動-數位輔助的實地探索。本課程將運用包含一個Web系統及數個APP的自製M-DCH平台”DEH”（http://deh.csie.ncku.edu.tw），進行M-DCH概論、DEH平台的使用、M-DCH內容創製與應用和專題製作/報告。  \nThis course’s theme is integrating IT technologies with culture heritage to have the Mobile Digital Culture Heritage (M-DCH). In contrast to the Digital Culture Heritage (DCH), which may emphasize on utilizing 2/3D animation technologies to have virtual exploring of culture heritage in a screen, M-DCH mainly emphasizes on walking into the sites of culture heritage by carrying with some handheld devices to have the physical exploring of culture heritage. That is, the purpose of M-DCH is to have the on-site exploring of the physical culture heritage through the wireless-mobile-digital assistance of some IT technologies. This course is based on the self-made M-DCH platform called Demodulating and Encoding Heritage (DEH) (http://deh.csie.ncku.edu.tw), which contains a web system and several APPs. Four parts of this course are (1) tutorial of M-DCH, (2) practice and usage of the DEH platform, (3) content creation and the potential applications of M-DCH using the DEH platform, (4) students’ presentations of their projects using the DEH platform.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   學習什麼是行動數位文化資產(M-DCH）\n*   了解M-DCH平台應提供的一般以及進階功能\n*   能夠使用實際的M-DCH平台來建立M-DCH內容以及其實務的應用功能\n*   了解M-DCH的潛在商轉營運模式\n*   跨領域知識學習及跨領域學生合作之訓練和經驗\n*   此為「踏溯2.0課程」，學生修習後，將了解如何轉換地方文化資產成行動數位內容。\n*   此課程為教育部「教學實踐研究計畫」補助，學生可實際體驗跨領域之翻轉教學。\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | M-DCH的簡介 |\n| 2 | M-DCH的後設資料格式、DEH Web內容下載/瀏覽與DEH APP-DEH Mini (戶外練習)之使用 |\n| 3 | DEH Web系統的M-DCH內容創作之使用 |\n| 4 | DEH APP-DEH Make之使用 |\n| 5 | DEH之進階功能-群組和特定場域功能 |\n| 6 | DEH之進階功能-文資學堂 |\n| 7 | 專題演講 (Invited Talk) |\n| 8 | M-DCH的潛在商轉營運模式 |\n| 9 | 學生之現地M-DCH內容創作 |\n| 10 | 與海佃國中學生進行合作之分組與設定專題二(期末專題)的場域/題目 |\n| 11 | 口頭報告(一): 專題一(期中專題)之成果展示 (Outdoor or indoor) |\n| 12 | 學生為專題二(期末專題)作準備 |\n| 13 | 口頭報告(二): 專題二(期末專題)之提案報告 |\n| 14 | 口頭報告(三): 專題三-與國內/外其它相關web系統/APPs (地圖故事, …)的比較及提出M-DCH的潛在營運模式之創新構想 |\n| 15 | 專題二(期末專題)之現地製作 |\n| 16 | 專題二(期末專題)之現地成果展示 (戶外) |\n| 17 | 口頭報告(四): DEH平台功能建議及與海佃國中學生協作之心得報告 |\n| 18 | 期末書面報告 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? It goes through building Knowledge system to field research and cases study, and aims to developthe appreciation of ethnic music. In order to advancing the ability of Reflection and contextually thinking way, this course reconstructs the history and cultural context of Taiwan's Indigenous peoples through designing questions and interviewing of field research. The course hopes to promote a participative action for the cultural revival of Indigenous peoples, hoping to help students improving the acceptance of Multiethnic, innovation of thinking way, and knowing the social responsibility.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   尊重與欣賞多元音樂藝術與文化價值\n*   應用田野調查研究法與訪談技巧\n*   關注原住民族在文化復振，反思自身可提供之貢獻\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介與分組，田野調查進行方式簡介，原住民這學期即將舉辦之祭典介紹 |\n| 2 | 南島語族與台灣原住民分佈 |\n| 3 | 台灣原住民族音樂傳統音樂鑑賞方式 |\n| 4 | 民族音樂田野調查一～音樂紀錄方式 |\n| 5 | 民族音樂田野調查二～訪談技巧與祭典紀錄方式 |\n| 6 | 民族音樂田野調查三～各組指導（一） |\n| 7 | 民族音樂田野調查三～各組指導（二） |\n| 8 | 原住民傳統生活與歌謠 |\n| 9 | 原住民傳統宗教信仰、儀式與舞樂與近代變遷 |\n| 10 | 期中報告：質性訪談實作與田野調查日誌（小組） |\n| 11 | 原住民歌謠變遷（一）悲歡離合的流浪者之歌 |\n| 12 | 原住民歌謠的變遷（二）：流行山地歌的美麗與哀愁 |\n| 13 | 非物質文化遺產公約～原住民傳統樂器介紹 |\n| 14 | 原住民歌謠的變遷（三）：原住民平權運動歌謠與議題探討 |\n| 15 | 口頭報告（一）阿美族 布農族 排灣族 魯凱族 撒奇萊雅族 |\n| 16 | 口頭報告（二）泰雅族 賽夏族 太魯閣族 賽德克族 葛瑪蘭族 邵族 |\n| 17 | 口頭報告（三） 西拉雅族 平埔族（馬卡道族 大武壟族 洪雅族 葛哈巫族 巴宰族） |\n| 18 | 口頭報告（四）卑南族 卡那卡那富族 鄒族 拉阿魯哇族 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   性別平等 (Gender Equality)\n*   和平與正義制度 (Peace justice and strong institutions)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 1 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? The United Nation’s Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) are a universal call to achieve a sustainable future and promote equality, human rights, and justice for all by 2030. Adopted by UN Member States in 2015, the 2030 Agenda for Sustainable Development provides a shared strategy for peace and prosperity for all people and our planet, now and into the future.     "課程大綱": "Title: 跨領域半導體產業概論FUNDAMENTALS OF CROSS-DOMAIN SEMICONDUCTOR INDUSTRY 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A93F600&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n■ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n□ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n□ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n□ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n■ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n■ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n■ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n這門課主要引導非理工背景學生認識半導體產業的發展脈絡，課程中將介紹半導體產業的發展與現狀，讓學生認識半導體產業的上中下游、市場發展、國際趨勢及未來科技整合等。本課程主要用意是希望非理工背景的學生，可藉由此課程所傳授的半導體產業知識，能夠更有機會加入積體電路相關的職場。  \nThis course mainly guides students from non-technical backgrounds to understand the development context of the semiconductor industry. The course will introduce the development and current situation of the semiconductor industry, so that students can understand the upstream, midstream and downstream, market development, international trends and future technology integration of the semiconductor industry. The main purpose of this course is to hope that students with non-technical backgrounds can have more opportunities to join the workplace related to integrated circuits through the knowledge of the semiconductor industry imparted by this course.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   理解半導體產業的歷史與未來發展趨勢\n*   分析全球半導體及相關產業的發展趨勢\n*   掌握半導體製造流程與技術知識\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程簡介:半導體產業生態系的前世,今生與未來 |\n| 2 | 全球電子產業供應鏈的管理,解構與重生 |\n| 3 | 全球人工智慧新創產業發展趨勢 |\n| 4 | 全球ESG發展趨勢與企業淨零碳排管理 |\n| 5 | (10/10 放假, 停課一次) |\n| 6 | 企業參訪(聯電智慧製造+半導體設備學院) |\n| 7 | 大師講座:我的半導體人生 |\n| 8 | IC製造概論(元件設計、晶圓製造、先進封裝) |\n| 9 | 潔淨能源與核融合發展趨勢 |\n| 10 | 半導體產業: EDA產業概論 |\n| 11 | 女力講座: 如何成為自己心目中的巨人 |\n| 12 | 半導體產業: 產品行銷與產業概論 |\n| 13 | 企業參訪(奇景光電 ) |\n| 14 | 半導體產業: IC設計與產業概論 (SoC) |\n| 15 | 全球ICT產業發展趨勢 |\n| 16 | 半導體產業 :第三代半導體應用與長期發展趨勢 |\n| 17 | 期末專題分組報告(專題研究結論,心得,反思與回饋.) |\n| 18 | (學期最後一週,,停課一次) |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n*   減少不平衡 (Reduced Inequalities)\n*   責任消費與生產 (Responsible consumption and production)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 4 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? How many times? Yes, about 4 times.  \n2.本課程是否規劃含校外實習(並非參訪)? 否  \nAre there any internships involved in the course? How many hours? No  \n3.本課程是否可歸認為學術倫理課程? 否  \nIs this course recognized as an academic ethics course? In the course how many hours are regarding academic ethics topics? No  \n4.本課程是否屬進入社區實踐課程? 否  \nIs this course recognized as a Community engagement and Service learning course? Which community will be engaged? No\n"

Environmental policy; 2. Environmental research; 3. Ecological engineering methods. Part II: Agriculture, life sciences and environmental conservation, including 1. Climate change and food security; 2. Environmental changes in extreme climates in Taiwan; 3. Sustainable agriculture. Part III: Law, environmental engineering and environmental conservation, including 1. Geological disaster; 2. Environmental protection and democratic participation; 3. Impact of pesticides: the truth behind the story. Part IV: Marine resources and environmental conservation, including 1, marine ecosystem; 2, estuary and coastal ecosystems; 3, oceanic and offshore ecosystems.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   理解周遭環境的生態多樣性與相關知識\n*   了解環境生態保育的重要性與實踐方法\n*   從自身的專業背景反思如何參與和貢獻\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹與規定說明 |\n| 2 | 專題演講：溪頭自然園區經營與生態保育(台大實驗林江博能研究員) |\n| 3 | 專題演講：馬頭山生態奇蹟與惡的距離(馬頭山自然人文協會黃惠敏理事長) |\n| 4 | 專題演講：綠能與台灣離岸風電的發展及環境議題(哥本哈根風能開發股份有限公司盧昱辰許可經理理) |\n| 5 | 國慶日 |\n| 6 | 心得檢討與反思(本校通識中心教學組長黃兆立) |\n| 7 | 專題演講：聚眾不滋事，公私協力以大數據改變環境--路殺社公民科學(農業部生多所林德恩研究員) |\n| 8 | 專題演講：未完成的夢--沙漠中的濕地(本校環工系黃榮振教授) |\n| 9 | 專題演講：你家變我家，垃圾變黃金--營建剩餘土石方之華麗轉身(本校土木系劉光晏教授) |\n| 10 | 心得檢討與反思(本校通識中心教學組長黃兆立) |\n| 11 | 專題演講：婆羅洲雨林野瘋狂(生態攝影家黃一峰先生) |\n| 12 | 專題演講：海洋保育三部曲--從取不盡用不竭到看見棺材也掉淚(嘉義大學生物資源系邱郁文教授) |\n| 13 | 專題演講：食魚教育(暫定；年年有鰆創辦人巫佳容小姐) |\n| 14 | 專題演講：海龜救傷中心在保育工作上的角色(海生館李宗賢研究員) |\n| 15 | 專題演講：待定 |\n| 16 | 專題演講：以海為題：書寫的溫柔之力(黑潮海洋文教基金會兼生態作家張卉君小姐) |\n| 17 | 心得檢討與反思(本校通識中心教學組長黃兆立) |\n| 18 | 期末報告寫作 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   氣候行動 (Climate action)\n*   海洋生態 (Life below water)\n*   陸地生態 (Life on land)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 3 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Leaving high school and going to college is complicated for everyone. This course is served as an introductory course for college freshmen to help them get adjusted into new life and environment. We will introduce the useful resource in NCKU, such as exchange program, scholarship, inter-disciplinary credit program. In this course, we will have mentors from various schools for students to choose. Mentors and mentees will have 5 weeks together to explore topics they are interested. Overall, this course would be a good guidance for freshmen to prepare and plan for a good college life.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   瞭解大學的意義與學習的方式\n*   了解成大的學習資源並規劃學習地圖及設定學習目標\n*   探索自我與情緒管理\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | 課程介紹、班級人員互動交流 |\n| 2 | 密集作業說明、作業1訪談之練習 |\n| 3 | 密集作業說明 |\n| 4 | 日常交通事例分析 |\n| 5 | 作業2閱讀作業 |\n| 6 | 學長姐來了 |\n| 7 | 金融管理學 |\n| 8 | 新科技與媒體著作權 |\n| 9 | Chat GPT (線上) |\n| 10 | 學習策略與延宕心理學 |\n| 11 | 閱讀俱樂部 (分組活動) |\n| 12 | 閱讀俱樂部 |\n| 13 | 校園心理健康、自殺防治(線上) |\n| 14 | 創新產業 |\n| 15 | 創新產業 |\n| 16 | 密集作業工作坊 |\n| 17 | 密集作業工作坊 |\n| 18 | 密集作業工作坊 |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   性別平等 (Gender Equality)\n*   就業與經濟成長 (Decent work and Economic growth)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   創新 Innovation\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 9 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Understand that our relationship learning from our original family has formed our relationship with ourselves, and then used it in interpersonal and intimacy consciously or unconsciously. 2. Explore the influence of the original family on oneself and the relationship, recognize and experience the \" survival stance\", connect with the \"self\" in the relationship, learn from the difference (appreciate each other's characteristics and resources), and explore one's own inner journey (\"iceberg theory), understand the interactive elements of the relationship. 3.     "課程大綱": "Title: 科學量化與政策制定SCIENCE QUANTIFICATION AND POLICY 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=A94F100&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 文化素養\n\nCultural Literacy\n\n□ 歷史意識\n\nHistorical awareness\n\n□ 藝術涵養\n\nArt and visual literacy\n\n■ 公民素養\n\nCivic literacy\n\n■ 國際視野\n\nGlobal Vision\n\n□ 生命關懷\n\nConcerns of Life\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n□ 語文欣賞及運用能力\n\nTo use language skills\n\n■ 慎思明辨能力\n\nTo think critically\n\n■ 跨領域能力\n\nTo cross disciplinary boundaries\n\n□ 社會變遷因應能力\n\nTo adapt to social change\n\n□ 生活實踐能力\n\nTo practice\n\n□ 創新與領導能力\n\nTo innovate and lead\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n\"科學支持政策制定\"是將資訊從科學界(個別研究人員、科學社群)傳遞給各級政策制定者，並納入以實證為政策基礎的過程。如今，無論涉及主題或政府層級，幾乎每一個立法都具有量化或半量化的科學元素。 儘管政策不單由科學制定，但科學可以幫助包括公眾在內的各級決策者，更準確地評估不同選項的優點和潛在後果。然而，這個過程存在技術及社會經濟為根本原因的重大挑戰和本質性不足。 對這些限制的明確認知以及對其正確的視覺呈現(包含對影響的視覺化)的日益關注，已在最近幾年內徹底改變了科學界。在大多數科技先進國家，科學家撰寫報告並(與社會)期望政策制定者會簡單地根據報告行事的日子已經不在。 本課程將邀請來自歐盟執委會數位總署講師，分享其在科學支持政策制定方面25多年工作期間的經驗和實際見解。本密集課程藉由分享不同應用領域的最新知識和最佳實踐範例，特別是從環境永續領域，將帶學生探索社會各方利害關係者(包括科學家和政策制定者)，可以更好地互動、建立信任和制定明智決策所需的技能。本課程講述利害關係者所需的技能，以使研究結果能夠對政策和社會產生更大的影響。  \nScience for Policy is the process by which information is transferred “from science” (individual researchers, scientific communities) to policymakers at all levels and incorporated into a process called evidence-based or evidence-informed policy. Nowadays, almost every legislative action, regardless of the topic or government level, has a scientific component to it, typically encoded in a quantitative or semi-quantitative manner. While policies are not made by science alone, science can help decision-makers at all levels, including the public, to more accurately assess the benefits and potential consequences of the different options available. – There are, however, significant challenges and deficits inherently related to this process, having technical and socio-economic root causes. The explicit recognition of these limitations and the growing interest in their proper visualisation, including visualisation of their impacts, have changed the scientific world beyond recognition in recent years. The days when scientists produced reports and expected, together with society, that policy-makers would simply act upon them are gone in most technologically developed countries. The course will invite a guest speaker to share his experience and practical insights accumulated over a career spanning over 25 years , encompassing work in both science support and policy-making services at the European Commission DG CONNECT. Through sharing of state-of-the art knowledge and best practice examples from different application areas, particularly from environmental sustainability, this module outlines the skills needed by stakeholders so that research results could have a bigger impact on policy and society in general. This course explores the skills which all stakeholders across society, including scientists and policy-makers, need in order to better engage with each other, build trust and develop informed decisions.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   科學支持政策制定- 使用不同語言、界線劃定\n*   實證基礎政策的概念- 歷史發展、科學危機、科學危機時期的科學諮詢挑戰\n*   基本工具：質量保證、同儕審查、不確定性/敏感性分析\n*   延伸工具：共同創造、擴展同儕審查、質量映射\n*   國際永續性政策的範例(發展、實施、監督)：過去 - 現在 - 可能的未來\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | INTRODUCTION TO THE COURSE – OBJECTIVE, SCOPE, CONCEPTS, FORMAT |\n| 2 | Exercise 1 |\n| 3 | SCIENCE ETHICS – AN INTRODUCTION |\n| 4 | Exercise 2 |\n| 5 | ETHICS ABOUT NUCLEAR POWER |\n| 6 | Exercise 3 |\n| 7 | WHY IS THERE A CRISIS OF SCIENCE? |\n| 8 | EVIDENCE BASED POLICY IN TIMES OF A CRISIS OF SCIENCE |\n| 9 | CONDITIONS AND LIMITS OF THE SCIENTIFIC METHOD |\n| 10 | Exercise 4 |\n| 11 | TRUST IN MODELS AND UNCERTAINTY/SENSITIVITY ANALYSIS |\n| 12 | Exercise 5 |\n| 13 | EX-ANTE EVALUATION AND COMPARING OPTIONS |\n| 14 | COMPOSITE INDICATORS TO EVALUATE/MONITOR OPTIONS |\n| 15 | EX-ANTE IMPACT ASSESSMENT AND EX-POST EVALUATION |\n| 16 | Exercise 6 |\n| 17 | REGULATORY CAPTURE / PRECAUTION VERSUS INNOVATION |\n| 18 | PERSONAL LESSONS LEARNED ON SCIENCE4POLICY AND CONCLUSIONS |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   可負擔能源 (Affordable and clean energy)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 是，約 3 次  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Introduction to Software Engineering and Project Development 2. Version Control in Project Development 3. Tasks in Mid-to-Large Scale Project 4. Unified Modeling Language 5. Model-View-Controller Architecture 6. Software Engineering Best Practices\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   網頁服務系統實作\n*   軟體工程實作練習\n*   系統重構能力\n*   code review\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Course Introduction |\n| 2 | Software Engineering Introduction + Clean Code Introduction |\n| 3 | Git + Docker |\n| 4 | Front\\_End 解說 ＋ Project說明 |\n| 5 | Meaningful Names + Comments |\n| 6 | Unit Tests |\n| 7 | Function Design |\n| 8 | Profiling Tools + Integration test |\n| 9 | how to use GPT |\n| 10 | Error/Exception Handling |\n| 11 | Objects and Data Structures + Classes |\n| 12 | Objects and Data Structures + Classes |\n| 13 | Software Engineering - SRS + Diagrams/ Refactor |\n| 14 | Design Pattern/ Refactor |\n| 15 | Build New Crawler / Refactor |\n| 16 | DevOps/ Refactor |\n| 17 | Refactor |\n| 18 | Final Demo |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   溝通表達 Communication and expression\n*   持續學習 Continuous learning\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n*   團隊合作 Teamwork\n*   人際互動 Interpersonal interaction\n*   資訊科技應用 Application of information technology\n*   工作責任及紀律 Job responsibilities and disciplines\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? This is a one or two semester course and covers the following topics: Mechanics, Thermal, Electricity & Magnetism, Optics, and Quantum Physics.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   基礎物理學概念的學習與科學方法培養\n*   學習基礎的力學、熱學概念\n*   提供學生於該科系領域或未來發展所需的物理基礎能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Measurement |\n| 2 | Motion along a Straight Line |\n| 3 | Vector |\n| 4 | Motion in Two and Three Dimensions |\n| 5 | Force and Motion |\n| 6 | Force and Motion |\n| 7 | Quiz |\n| 8 | Kinetic Energy and Work |\n| 9 | Potential Energy and Conservation of Energy |\n| 10 | Center of Mass and Linear Momentum |\n| 11 | Rotation |\n| 12 | Rolling, Torque, and Angular Momentum |\n| 13 | Quiz |\n| 14 | Equilibrium and Elasticity |\n| 15 | Gravitation |\n| 16 | Fluids |\n| 17 | Oscillations |\n| 18 | Final exam |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程是否與永續發展目標相關調查  \nSurvey of the conntent relevant to SDGs\n---------------------------------------------------------\n\n本課程與SDGs相關項目如下：  \nThis course is relevant to these items of SDGs as following:\n\n*   教育品質 (Quality Education)\n*   工業、創新與基礎建設 (Industry Innovation and infrastructure)\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n*   問題解決 Problem solving\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Description\n-----------------------\n\n透過本課程，使學生親身體會服務學習的意涵及重要性；並培養對其分內工作之責任感以及學習與工作夥伴溝通之能力。  \n透過本課程，使學生親身體會服務學習的意涵及重要性；並培養對其分內工作之責任感以及學習與工作夥伴溝通之能力。\n\n課程學習目標 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\n1\\. 延續大一微積分基礎，介紹工程問題上，較常使用微分方程式的數學解析方法。 2. 探討如何利用拉普拉斯轉換將微分方程式的數學模式，轉換為代數型式，進而利用四則運算快速求解。 3 探討如何利用於特定點的級數解，分析微分方程式，進而介紹二個特別的數學函數。 4 透過實例介紹讓同學了解描述各類變量關係的一些微分方程式或分析變量關係的一些數學方法。  \n1.First-Order Differential Equations2.Linear Differential Equations of Second and Higher Order3.Systems of Differential Equations, Phase Plane, Qualitative Methods4.Series Solutions of Differential Equations. Special Functions5.Laplace Transform6.Fourier Series, Integral, and Transforms7.Numerical Methods for Differential Equations8.Differential Equations with MATLAB.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   了解微分程式\n*   了解Laplace transform\n*   了解 series solution\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | First-Order Ordinary Differential Equations (ODEs) |\n| 2 | Integrating Factors |\n| 3 | Linear ODEs, Bernoulli Equation |\n| 4 | Second-Order Linear ODEs, Homogeneous Linear ODEs |\n| 5 | Homogeneous Linear ODEs with Constant Coefficients |\n| 6 | Differential Operators, Euler-Cauchy Equations |\n| 7 | Wronskian, Nonhomogeneous ODEs, Solution by Variation of Parameters |\n| 8 | Midterm |\n| 9 | Laplace Transform basic property |\n| 10 | Laplace Transform of basic functions |\n| 11 | The first shifting theoremThe second shifting theorem |\n| 12 | Other special properties of Laplace Transform |\n| 13 | Ordinary points, Regular singular points, Irregular singular points |\n| 14 | Taylor series expansion, Frobenius series, Indicial equation, |\n| 15 | Legendre’s function, Bessel function |\n| 16 | Final examination |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? As open-source software, the Linux-based systems have been used in a variety of computer systems, ranging from cellphones to data centers. The aim of this course is to make the students be familiar with the Linux environments. After a brief introduction of the major hardware components in commodity PCs, we will talk about the basic concepts/tools that could be used in open-source projects, such as version control systems, text editor, shell scripting, and makefile. In addition, we will introduce the basis of Linux system management, regarding software packages, running processes, networking, and performance analysis. Finally, we will cover the advanced topics from the system software perspective, including inter-process communication, namespace, Cgroups, and Docker. Each class session is divided into two parts: lecturing and hands-on lab.  \nLinux is one of the most popular Unix-like operating systems in the world. As open-source software, the Linux-based systems have been used in a variety of computer systems, ranging from cellphones to data centers. The aim of this course is to make the students be familiar with the Linux environments. After a brief introduction of the major hardware components in commodity PCs, we will talk about the basic concepts/tools that could be used in open-source projects, such as version control systems, text editor, shell scripting, and makefile. In addition, we will introduce the basis of Linux system management, regarding software packages, running processes, networking, and performance analysis. Finally, we will cover the advanced topics from the system software perspective, including inter-process communication, namespace, Cgroups, and Docker. Each class session is divided into two parts: lecturing and hands-on lab.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   教育學生具備資訊專業知識及終身學習之能力\n*   教育學生具備獨立研究、設計及創新之能力\n*   教育學生優質團隊合作及國際觀之能力\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Introduction |\n| 2 | Basics of hardware platform for Linux systems |\n| 3 | Version control system: Git |\n| 4 | Vim and its plug-in |\n| 5 | Bash and Shell Scripts |\n| 6 | Makefile and Maven |\n| 7 | Linux command-line tools |\n| 8 | Review and discussion |\n| 9 | Package management |\n| 10 | Process management |\n| 11 | Networking |\n| 12 | Basics of performance analysis |\n| 13 | Tools for performance analysis |\n| 14 | Inter-process communication |\n| 15 | Robotic Operating Systems (ROS) |\n| 16 | ROS-based autonomous driving systems |\n| 17 | Simulated autonomous driving systems |\n| 18 | Review and discussion |\n\n以上每週進度教師可依上課情況做適度調整。The schedule may be subject to change.\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講? 否  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Academic Integrity and Ethics. 6. In this course, you’ll learn how to design user-centered experiments, how to run such experiments, and how to analyze data from these experiments in order to evaluate and validate user experiences. You will work through real-world examples of experiments from the fields of UX, IxD, and HCI, understanding issues in experiment design and analysis. You will analyze multiple data sets using recipes given to you in the R statistical programming language -- no prior programming experience is assumed or required, but you will be required to read, understand, and modify code snippets provided to you. By the end of the course, you will be able to knowledgeably design, run, and analyze your own experiments that give statistical weight to your designs.  \nYou may never be sure whether you have an effective user experience until you have tested it with users. In this course, you’ll learn how to design user-centered experiments, how to run such experiments, and how to analyze data from these experiments in order to evaluate and validate user experiences. ANOVA and ANCOVA, presented as a type of linear regression model, will provide the mathematical basis for designing experiments for data science applications. Emphasis will be placed on important design-related concepts, such as randomization, blocking, factorial design, and causality. Some attention will also be given to ethical issues raised in experimentation.\\\\n\\\\nThis course can be taken for academic credit as part of CU Boulder’s Master of Science in Data Science (MS-DS) degree offered on the Coursera platform. The MS-DS is an interdisciplinary degree that brings together faculty from CU Boulder’s departments of Applied Mathematics, Computer Science, Information Science, and others. With performance-based admissions and no application process, the MS-DS is ideal for individuals with a broad range of undergraduate education and/or professional experience in computer science, information science, mathematics, and statistics. Learners will discover a variety of techniques that can be used to represent sports data and how to extract narratives based on these analytical techniques. The main focus of the introduction will be on the use of regression analysis to analyze team and player performance data, using examples drawn from the National Football League (NFL), the National Basketball Association (NBA), the National Hockey League (NHL), the English Premier LEague (EPL, soccer) and the Indian Premier League (IPL, cricket). \\\\n\\\\nThis course does not simply explain methods and techniques, it enables the learner to apply them to sports datasets of interest so that they can generate their own results, rather than relying on the data processing performed by others. As a consequence the learning will be empowered to explore their own ideas about sports team performance, test them out using the data, and so become a producer of sports analytics rather than a consumer.\\\\n\\\\nWhile the course materials have been developed using Python, code has also been produced to derive all of the results in R, for those who prefer that environment.  \nThis course provides an introduction to using Python to analyze team performance in sports. Learners will discover a variety of techniques that can be used to represent sports data and how to extract narratives based on these analytical techniques.     "課程大綱": "Title: 應用TensorFlow 2客制化資料模型 IIPROBABILISTIC DEEP LEARNING WITH TENSORFLOW 2 本資訊僅提供本校師生參考。有著作權，非本校人員若欲使用本資訊，請洽本校取得授權。 © (2008-2024) National Cheng Kung University ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.\n\nURL Source: https://class-qry.acad.ncku.edu.tw/syllabus/syllabus.php?syear=0113&sem=1&co_no=F724700&class_code=\n\nMarkdown Content:\n基本素養 Basic Literacy\n-------------------\n\n□ 畢業生應具備科技人文素養及資訊工程倫理之精神\n\ngraduates should equip with both the attitude of technological/cultural literacy and the consciousness of information engineering ethics\n\n■ 畢業生應具備良好溝通技巧及國際觀\n\ngraduates should equip with appropriate communication skill and global view\n\n核心能力 Competence\n---------------\n\n■ 畢業生應具備基礎專業數學及資訊理論知識之基本能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the basic capability of the fundamental of professional mathematics and theoretical knowledge in informatics\n\n□ 畢業生應具備資訊理論推導及實驗設計、數據分析歸納之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the capability of information theory derivation、experiment design and experimental data analysis/induction\n\n□ 畢業生應具備培養學習興趣及持續學習之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the capability of learning interest development and continuous learning\n\n□ 畢業生應具備獨立、創新思維及發掘、分析、解決資訊相關問題之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the capability to think creatively and independently and to explore, analyze, and solve information-related problems\n\n□ 畢業生應具備資訊系統設計、測試及驗證之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the information system ability in designing and verification\n\n□ 畢業生應具備資訊系統整合之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with the capability of system integration\n\n□ 畢業生應具備負責之工作態度及有效團隊合作之能力\n\ngraduates should equip with a responsible attitude in working and the capability of effective team-work collaboration\n\n□ 具備有效溝通表達的專業語文能力\n\n課程概述 Course Description\n-----------------------\n\nThis course builds on the foundational concepts and skills for TensorFlow taught in the first two courses in this specialisation, and focuses on the probabilistic approach to deep learning. This is an increasingly important area of deep learning that aims to quantify the noise and uncertainty that is often present in real world datasets. This is a crucial aspect when using deep learning models in applications such as autonomous vehicles or medical diagnoses; we need the model to know what it doesn't know. You will learn how to develop probabilistic models with TensorFlow, making particular use of the TensorFlow Probability library, which is designed to make it easy to combine probabilistic models with deep learning. As such, this course can also be viewed as an introduction to the TensorFlow Probability library. You will learn how probability distributions can be represented and incorporated into deep learning models in TensorFlow, including Bayesian neural networks, normalising flows and variational autoencoders. You will learn how to develop models for uncertainty quantification, as well as generative models that can create new samples similar to those in the dataset, such as images of celebrity faces. You will put concepts that you learn about into practice straight away in practical, hands-on coding tutorials, which you will be guided through by a graduate teaching assistant. In addition there is a series of automatically graded programming assignments for you to consolidate your skills. At the end of the course, you will bring many of the concepts together in a Capstone Project, where you will develop a variational autoencoder algorithm to produce a generative model of a synthetic image dataset that you will create yourself.  \nThis course builds on the foundational concepts and skills for TensorFlow taught in the first two courses in this specialisation, and focuses on the probabilistic approach to deep learning. This is an increasingly important area of deep learning that aims to quantify the noise and uncertainty that is often present in real world datasets. In addition there is a series of automatically graded programming assignments for you to consolidate your skills. At the end of the course, you will bring many of the concepts together in a Capstone Project, where you will develop a variational autoencoder algorithm to produce a generative model of a synthetic image dataset that you will create yourself.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? It contains three modules: (i) basic statistical inferences, (ii) design of experiment and experimental data analysis and (iii) linear regression and advanced regression methods. After this course, students shall gain principle understandings for basic statistical design / modeling / learning / analysis and are able to perform proper inferences for fundamental statistical models.  \nThis course is an introduction to the mathematical theory of statistical learning. It contains three modules: (i) basic statistical inferences, (ii) design of experiment and experimental data analysis and (iii) linear regression and advanced regression methods. After this course, students shall gain principle understandings for basic statistical design / modeling / learning / analysis and are able to perform proper inferences for fundamental statistical models.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n課程與職場共通職能關聯程度調查  \nSurvey of the course content relevant to Workplace Competencies\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n有關課程其他調查 Other Surveys of Courses\n---------------------------------\n\n1.本課程是否規劃業界教師參與教學或演講?  \nIs there any industry specialist invited in this course? Description\n-----------------------\n\n這門課上半學期授課將以老師的講義配合OpenCV教科書所提供較實用的程式功能論述為主，下半學期將以老師深度學習講義為主來授課。 課程內容將以常會用到的影像處理、電腦視覺及人工智慧-深度學習的理論基礎及技術為主，並學習及實作OpenCV的功能與實務應用。為了讓學生了解深度學習網絡架構設計的原理是如何結合人工智慧類神經網路及電腦視覺發展而來的相互關係，課程中會傳授影像處理中最重要的 convolution 基本原理與實際應用，並會讓學生了解如何用神經網路來實現並強化 convolution 的功能以完善 Convolutional Neural Networks (CNN) 的架構 (topology)。講解的方法將融入老師20幾年的產學合作經驗（臉部偵測、辨識及表情分析、雲端智慧型監控服務、自動光學檢測、智慧製造、智慧型機器手臂控制、自走車）及近年來在臨床醫學影像與精準運動科技經驗來舉實際的範例解釋基礎原理，透過這些理論來解決實際的問題；技術內容包括影像處理、電腦視覺 （即時偵測、追蹤及辨識模組的設計、3D立體視覺、增擬實境）及深度學習等等。 本課程期待培養學生於影像處理、電腦視覺及深度學習領域技術設計及整合實作的能力，透過務實的作業實例來培育學生具備研發思考、程式設計及解決現存問題的能力，藉由分組計畫的實作來培養學生具備發現問題、解決問題及團隊分工合作的能力與精神，並可把所學的理論基礎應用到工業界智慧製造自動化、臨床醫學影像處理及精準運動科技的實務面。  \nThis class will focus on the teacher's lecture notes and the more practical functional arguments (function calls) provided by the OpenCV textbook for the first half of the semester about OpenCV. The teacher's lecture notes will be used for the second half of the semester about deep learning. The content of the course will focus on the theoretical basis and practical techniques of image processing, computer vision and artificial intelligence – deep learning. OpenCV functions and practical applications will also be learnt. In order to let students understand how the principles of depth learning combine artificial neural networks (ANNs) and the interrelationships of computer vision, the most important principles and practical applications of image processing – convolution will be taught. Therefore, students will be able to understand how to implement and enhance the functionality of the convolution in order to perfect the architecture of Convolutional Neural Networks (CNN). In addition, the lectures will incorporate teacher’s more than 20 years of experience in industrial cooperation (face detection, recognition and expression analysis, intelligent video surveillance as a service, automated optical inspection (AOI), intelligent manufacturing, visual-guided robot arm control, and automatic guided vehicle (AGV)) and recent practical examples of clinical imaging and AI Sports to explain the fundamentals and solve practical problems through these theories, including image processing, computer vision (real-time detection, tracking and recognition, 3D stereo or visualization, augmented reality (AR)) and deep learning. This course looks forward to developing students' ability to design and integrate practical skills in image processing, computer vision and depth learning, and to develop students' R&D thinking, programming design, and practical consideration through practical practice in order to have the ability to solve existing problems. Through the practical work of group project, students' ability and spirit of discovering problems, solving problems and team work-sharing can be nurtured. They can also apply the theoretical foundation to industry, clinical imaging and precision sports analytics.\n\n課程學習目標 Course Objectives\n------------------------\n\n*   具備基本的影像處理、電腦視覺及深度學習理論基礎；\n*   融匯貫通深度學習的原理是如何結合人工智慧、電腦視覺及影像處理。\n*   具備以電腦視覺及深度學習的技術來解決即時偵測、追蹤、辨識及增擬實境的實際問題。\n*   學習OpenCV的功能原理及實務應用。\n\n課程進度 Progress Description\n-------------------------\n\n|  | 進度說明 Progress Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| 1 | Introduction to Image Processing and OpenCV |\n| 2 | Holiday |\n| 3 | Image processing 1 - Image transforms: Hough transformation, geometric trans., FT (Fourier transform), II (integral image) and histogram equalization. |\n| 6 | Image processing 2 - Image transforms: Hough transformation, geometric trans., FT (Fourier transform), II (integral image) and histogram equalization. |\n| 7 | Image proc. 3 – (Texture) Histograms and matching: Stochastic and probability. |\n| 8 | Image proc. 3 – (Texture) Histograms and matching: Stochastic and probability. |\n| 9 | Image processing 4 – (Shape) Contours: Data structure -
